Chapter 251: Arhat Fist

“Come, assume the horse stance. Get in position, and start learning the Arhat Fist.”

Lu Yang followed Meng Jingzhou’s movements. Letting his qi sink to his dantian, he puffed his chest and lifted his head. His left foot took half a step to the left, while both palms traced arcs.

“Ha!”

“You aren’t loud enough! Again!”

“Ha!”

“Louder!”

“Ha!”

Lu Yang shouted louder and louder, until he finally met Meng Jingzhou’s standards.

“Shifu taught me that yelling in battle is a way to release restraints. The louder you shout, the more you can unleash your true strength, surpassing your usual power.

“When throwing a punch, make sure to keep your arms and line of sight level.

“Your fist must be tight. Imagine holding a stone in your hand and squeezing it with all your might, as if you’re trying to crush it.”

These were the lessons Meng Jingzhou had learned from Third Elder, and he was now passing them on to Lu Yang.

“Arhat Fist emphasizes coordination between the upper and lower body, with the feet following the hands. You must achieve a balance between firmness and softness. Your movements are too stiff; they need to flow and be gentler!”

Meng Jingzhou pointed out Lu Yang’s mistakes one by one and corrected him. These were common errors when practicing fist techniques.

Lu Yang was talented in martial arts, which was evident from how he learned the Animal Form Fist in just half a day and then enhanced it into the Lu-Style Animal Form Fist within the remaining half of the day.

“The sea of suffering is endless; turning back leads to the shore!” Lu Yang picked up the form quickly, his countenance reflecting the compassion of a monk.

Lu Yang’s ears rang with Meng Jingzhou’s earnest teachings. “Shifu told me that the Arhat Fist is a fist technique for guiding people toward goodness. The saying ‘The sea of suffering is endless; turning back leads to the shore’ means that if a person can put down their weapons of slaughter and turn toward goodness through practicing the whole sequence, they would have achieved a major success with the Arhat Fist.

“Unfortunately, most people are ignorant. They are unable to lay down their weapons and focus on goodness. As such, not more than three people have mastered the Arhat Fist with major success.” Meng Jingzhou placed one hand over his chest, his posture somewhat exuding the aura of a senior monk.

“When learning Arhat Fist, your mindset is also very crucial. It’s best to imagine yourself as a disciple of Buddhism. In my case, I even studied Buddhist scriptures for a while.”

“Memorize and recite Buddhist scriptures?” Lu Yang faintly felt that he had found a way.

He didn’t need to start learning Buddhist scriptures now. Back when he was in the scripture library, he had read Buddhist scriptures such as The Diamond Sutra, The Vidyaraja[1] Sutra, and The Heart Sutra in his free time. They were incredibly effective at lulling him into hypnosis.

Slowly closing his eyes, the delicate face of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy surfaced in his mind. She was wearing a millet-yellow nightgown, tilting her head as her eyes met with Lu Yang.

“...Immortal Fairy, can you stand to the side of my mental space? I’m trying to recall Buddhist scriptures.”

“Oh.”

With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy gone from his vision, Lu Yang began to browse his memories, the contents of The Diamond Sutra, The Vidyaraja Sutra, and the Heart Sutra emerging before his eyes. He tried to contemplate and understand the mindsets of the authors by placing himself in their shoes.

In the real world, Meng Jingzhou was staring at Lu Yang in astonishment.

Lu Yang’s eyes were tightly closed. His movements were slower than before, resembling a withered old man, but every action of his carried the compassionate air of a senior monk.

Meng Jingzhou wondered, Could this fellow Lu Yang be suited to become a monk?

As Lu Yang’s comprehension of the Buddhist scriptures and Arhat Fist deepened, his movements became increasingly smooth, flowing like the river and not stopping a single moment. It was as though he had practiced these motions hundreds or thousands of times until they were now second nature.

Bang—bang—

Every punch Lu Yang threw was accompanied by the sound of air erupting and the faint echoes of a Buddhist chant, as if an old monk was reciting scriptures in the void to teach the world to show others kindness.

Lu Yang continued practicing with his eyes closed, from morning until evening. Seeing that there was nothing more to teach, Meng Jingzhou squatted at the side and waited for Lu Yang to finally open his eyes.

“Whew.” After completing a set, Lu Yang exhaled deeply and opened his eyes, which now sparkled brightly with energy.

“You mastered it?” Meng Jingzhou stared at Lu Yang in disbelief. It’d taken me three full days to learn it, but this kid did it in less than a day?

Is there still fairness in this world?

“Somewhat successful,” Lu Yang said modestly.

“Let’s try it out.” Meng Jingzhou was itching to test the results of Lu Yang’s training. I have learned this for more than half a month. I refuse to believe I can’t beat Lu Yang, who has only learned it for a day.

“Let’s try it then.” Lu Yang was also itching to gauge his level.

The two exchanged a glance and simultaneously assumed their stances, ready to compete with their Arhat Fist.

“Black Tiger Heart Strike!”

“Black Tiger Heart Strike!”

“Downward Smashing Hammer!”

“Downward Smashing Hammer!”

Their fists and feet collided with tremendous force like bolts of thunder in the training ground, shaking the surrounding trees until their leaves rustled.

Exchanging identical moves with equal strength, they enjoyed a thrilling battle, though it would take a while for the outcome to be decided.

“Who would have thought? You learned it in less than a day, and you’ve already mastered the fundamentals of Arhat Fist just like me. Maybe one day you’ll perfect it with major success and guide people toward goodness!”

“It was just a fluke.” Despite Lu Yang’s answer, the smug look on his face showed that luck had nothing to do with it.

Lu Yang wanted to feign modesty again when he inadvertently caught a glimpse of the top of Meng Jingzhou’s head, and his expression changed subtly.

“What’s wrong? Is there something wrong with my head?” Meng Jingzhou was befuddled.

“No-nothing.” Lu Yang averted his eyes, as if he had a guilty conscience.

Meng Jingzhou eyed Lu Yang suspiciously and subconsciously touched his head. Hold on, is something missing from my head?

“Where’s my hair?!”

Meng Jingzhou whipped out a small mirror from his identity jade tablet and examined his head for a long time.

His head was so smooth that even a sparrow would slip on it.

He had gone bald.

New novel chapters are published on freeweɓnøvel.com.

Like an arhat monk.

Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was rolling on the floor laughing.

Meng Jingzhou’s first instinct was to suspect Lu Yang. “Lu Yang, you better explain to me what happened!” My hair is part of my refined body, so how could it have fallen out for no reason?

Then, he noticed hair all around his feet—they had just fallen off.

“I...I don’t know... I noticed your hair falling out really quickly when we were practicing fists just now. Just as I wanted to remind you, all of it was already gone.” Lu Yang panicked. He genuinely had no idea what had gone wrong.

Suddenly, Lu Yang seemed to have come to a realization. “I understand now.”

“What did you understand?”

“Think about it, isn’t the purpose of the Arhat Fist to guide people to goodness? And where does evil come from? From worries. In Buddhism, there’s a saying about three thousand hair strands of worries. Without these hair strands of worries, there’ll be no more evil, and people can turn toward goodness.”

“Besides, your current appearance looks so much like an arhat monk. It’s a perfect match with the Arhat Fist!”

Hearing his words, Meng Jingzhou immediately lunged at Lu Yang like a hungry tiger pouncing on its prey. “I think you are the one who looks like an arhat!”

Lu Yang felt guilty and bolted right away. “I have achieved major success with the Arhat Fist. You can’t hit me!”

“This isn’t Arhat Fist at all! It’s a head-shaving technique! Stop right there!”

1. The Wisdom King or literally “Bright King” in Chinese. ☜

Chapter 252: Yet You Say You’re Not A Monk

Four days passed quickly. The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes gathered at the city gate as agreed, though they were stunned upon seeing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“Young Heroes, where is your hair?” The hook-nosed boss blurted out when he noticed there wasn’t a single strand of hair on their heads. The moment the question slipped out, he regretted it.

The two people’s faces visibly darkened.

Meng Jingzhou’s hair had yet to grow back, and it would take at least a few more days. To apologize and appease Meng Jingzhou’s anger, Lu Yang could only shave his own head as well. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t stop laughing throughout the past few days.

The hook-nosed boss speculated, Could these two young heroes be disciples of a Buddhist sect? Perhaps they’ve been wearing wigs all this time?

The more he thought about it, the more convinced he became. The two of them haven’t mentioned their backgrounds, and it’s likely because they’re from a Buddhist sect; these Buddhist sects tend to keep a low profile.

Now that they have to fight for the Twin Lotus Flower, they need not only martial power but also the power of their identity to intimidate others!

As for slaying and eating demon beasts, that is also understandable. There are monks like the Fleshly Monk in Buddhist sects. They may be few, but they do exist.

“Let’s go,” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou gruffly, not wanting to explain further.

~~~

Following the map provided by the merchant guild, the group soon arrived at the lake where the Twin Lotus Flower grew.

The area around the lake was already teeming with people. Briefly scanning the place, they found hardly anyone at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage. The majority were at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, followed by those at the Golden Core Stage.

Due to the Twin Lotus Flower’s miraculous effects on golden core formation, it had attracted many cultivators seeking to break through to the Golden Core Stage. But it was hardly useful for Golden Core cultivators. Otherwise, having only a fish as lake master wouldn’t have been able to guard the Twin Lotus Flowers.

In the center of the lake, two lotus flower buds were about to bloom. All eyes were fixed on the pink and tender flowers that resembled twins.

“With all this water here, it will be difficult to fight when it’s time to seize the flowers.” An Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivator frowned. He wasn’t adept at water combat. If there were opponents who specialized in water-type spells, he would be at a disadvantage.

“Let’s drain the water.” He took out a storage ring and tried his best to fill it with the water from the lake.

When others saw what he did, they thought it was a good idea and followed suit. Since storage rings could only hold non-living objects, they were perfect for storing water without any living creatures from the lake.

“He is the White Tiger Holy Son from the Four-Divine-Beasts[1] Sect! It’s said that he has mastered a killing technique, and though he’s only at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage, he can hold his own against a Half-Step Golden Core cultivator!” The hook-nosed boss had been busy these few days, investigating who might come to fight for the Twin Lotus Flower.

The White Tiger Holy Son was one of them.

The Four-Divine-Beasts Sect was a prestigious first-class sect, renowned for its legacy of the Four Divine Beasts. It had outstanding disciples and successors in every generation and rarely experienced decline.

The Central Continent had a habit of classifying sects into different tiers. Those without a cultivator at the Divine Transfiguration Stage were considered low-tier sects and ranked at the very bottom.

Next were third-class sects, which had at least one cultivator at the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

Second-class sects had at least one cultivator at the Void Refinement Stage.

First-class sects had at least one cultivator at the Fusion Stage.

S-class sects had a formidable cultivator at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

Above the S-class sects were the Five Great Immortal Sects. Although the official benchmark to be recognized as one of the Five Great Immortal Sects required at least one Transcendent Tribulation cultivator and methods on par with that of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, the number of hidden trump cards they had remained anyone’s guess.

“Then there’s that female cultivator, An Ke, the final disciple of the sect leader of the Clear Moon Sect. She is at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage and the strongest among those at her level in the sect. Even the sect leader said he would be no match for An Ke if he were at the same cultivation stage.”

It was rumored in the jianghu that the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace was behind the Clear Moon Sect, though no one had been able to confirm it.

“The person over there is the Heaven Inquiry Saber, Duan Hongchen.[2] He has slain countless Golden Core beasts, and people thought he’d already reached the Golden Core Stage. But in reality, he is just at the Half-Step Golden Core Stage and has been looking for a suitable fortuitous opportunity to form his golden core!”

The hook-nosed boss pointed out the noteworthy individuals one by one. Some came from powerful sects and clans with impressive legacies, while others were locals of the Demon Suppression Pass who had earned their fame through bloodshed.

In comparison, hardly anyone knew about Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. They had only arrived at the Demon Suppression Pass a few days ago, living in the jungle and avoiding contact with people.

“Who are those two monks? Are they disciples of the White Horse Temple[3] or the Buddhist Stupa Temple?” Someone noticed Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. As the only two bald people in the crowd, they were especially conspicuous.

The White Tiger Holy Son frowned. “I’ve visited the White Horse Temple and Buddhist Stupa Temple with my shifu, but I’ve never seen these two.”

“Wild monks? Or are they from some unknown temple?” a member of the Four-Divine-Beasts Sect remarked. He always considered sects below first-class to be unworthy of his attention.

This chapter is updated by freēwēbnovel.com.

An Ke was expressionless, simply glancing at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou from the corner of her eye. Not matching them to any of the Foundation Establishment experts she remembered, she didn’t bother with them.

The Heaven Inquiry Saber, Duan Hong Chen, saw that the two were merely at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage and completely ignored them. My opponents are only those Golden Core cultivators hiding among the crowd.

These Golden Core cultivators here to snatch the Twin Lotus Flowers were mainly doing so to help their juniors break through to the Golden Core Stage, so they wouldn’t go all out. If it came to a life-or-death battle, they would be the first to withdraw.

When Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou overheard the others guessing which Buddhist sect they belonged to, veins bulged on their foreheads. You are the monk! Your whole family are monks!

“It’s all your fault for insisting that I shave my head!” Lu Yang was the first to lash out.

Meng Jingzhou was well-prepared. “You’re blaming me? It’s clearly because your version of the Arhat Fist was totally off-kilter! Just wait, I’ll write a letter recommending you to join the Hanging Monastery!”

With Lu Yang’s talents, he was qualified to join the Hanging Monastery, or perhaps, it was possible the Hanging Monastery would even warmly welcome him with open arms. After all, they can’t find a second person whose talent in spells is comparable to Big Senior Sister’s.

“Lu Yang, are you planning to become a monk?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was reluctant to see him go.

“No, the Dao-Seeking Sect is my home. I’m not going anywhere!” Lu Yang made his stance clear. I’ll live as a member of the Dao-Seeking Sect and die as a ghost of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Look! The lotus flowers are about to bloom!” someone shouted, attracting everyone’s attention.

The Twin Lotus Flower blossomed, releasing a refreshing fragrance that incited a frenzy as everyone rushed to seize it.

With the roar of a tiger, the White Tiger Holy Son acted first. A “王” character slowly appeared on his forehead.[4] White fur sprouted on his cheeks, and his pupils turned vertical, resembling a tiger.

“The Twin Lotus Flower is mine! No one else can take it!” He roared, moving as fast as the wind.

“You think it’s yours just because you say it is? Arhat Fist!” Meng Jingzhou attacked with the Arhat Fist. His countenance was wreathed in a compassion that bemoaned the pitiful state of mankind. One couldn’t execute such a fist technique without at least twenty years of experience as a monk.

The punch was absurdly heavy, pounding the White Tiger Holy Son into a daze and sending him crashing into the mud. This was the first time he failed when challenging an opponent beyond his level. All his battles were against opponents at a higher level, and he easily defeated Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivators despite being only at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage.

I didn’t expect I’d lose this time.

“As I thought, you’re a monk!” An Ke affirmed her earlier conjecture.

“You are the monk!” Meng Jingzhou snapped back.

“Bald, Arhat Fist—yet you say you’re not a monk?”

1. As mentioned in an earlier chapter (CH66), the Sixiang refers to the four divine beasts. ☜

2. The name sounds exactly like the phrase which means cutting oneself away from the mundane world and worldly affairs. ☜

3. The Baima Temple in Luoyang is one of the earliest Buddhist temples in China. ☜

4. It’s quite common in drawings of tigers by Chinese artists. ☜

Chapter 253: A Gathering of Buddhist Sects

The Twin Lotus Flower was pivotal to the formation of one’s golden core—no one would back down. Numerous Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivators clashed in a chaotic battle.

The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes were self-aware. Their skills might be sufficient for surviving in the jungle, but not for a direct confrontation with others. Furthermore, having witnessed the combat prowess of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, they doubted anyone could beat them.

Whenever cultivators defeat an opponent a minor cultivation stage higher, they can boast about it for half a day, as though it is a monumental achievement. In contrast, these two monks can challenge opponents a major cultivation stage higher and claim victory consecutively. Such combat power has only existed in rumors until now.

“Could they be from the Hanging Monastery?”

“The Hanging Monastery recruiting two people at once?”

“Judging by the skills of these two young heroes, it’s not impossible.”

As the second in his cohort, Meng Jingzhou was somewhat equivalent to being second among his cohort across the Five Great Immortal Sects. With such extraordinary combat strength, he naturally drew attacks from many cultivators. Even Golden Core cultivators could discern his aptitude and joined forces to take him down.

“Damn Lu Yang, don’t just watch from the sidelines!” Meng Jingzhou hollered for Lu Yang to help while using the Arhat Fist.

“I thought Great Hero Meng could take on a hundred by himself,” Lu Yang teased as he geared up for battle.

Four Advanced Foundation Establishment Cultivators teamed up to attack Lu Yang, but he barely glanced at them. With a sidestep, he dodged their strikes effortlessly, gently tapping their stomachs with the back of his hand. They immediately felt a sharp pang in their bellies and began vomiting uncontrollably.

“Ugh...”

“Quick, stop him!” The crowd realized that Lu Yang was not inferior to Meng Jingzhou and posed a major threat in this competition.

“Mountain-Shattering Palm!” Another cultivator attacked Lu Yang with iron-colored palms hardened by a thousand refinements. The skin was as tough as iron, and even a furnace would be unlikely to smelt them.

“Draw Underground Prison!” Lu Yang drew a circle on the ground with his finger.

The assailant suddenly vanished and sank underground, as if an invisible hand had forcibly dragged him down.

Such a bizarre method sent chills down everyone’s spine, leaving them clueless about how to respond.

“Successor of the Painting Dao?!” someone exclaimed, recognizing that Lu Yang’s technique was reminiscent of the Confucian cultivators proficient in the Dao of Painting. With one casual stroke, these people can turn heaven and earth upside down!

Isn’t this person a disciple of a Buddhist sect? How could he have performed Confucian techniques?

Lu Yang simply smiled, offering no explanation. He continued drawing circles as he faced the onslaught from the encirclement of cultivators, as though he was sauntering carefreely in a no-man’s land. Anyone who got too close to him was sent straight into the underground prison.

“Have a taste of my saber! Heaven Inquiry!” Duan Hongchen secretly struck from the shadows, his Heaven Inquiry Saber gleaming so brightly that it blinded the eyes of onlookers.

“Arhat Fist!” Lu Yang crouched slightly on his right leg and kept his left leg taut. His power surged through him, finally converging in his left fist. Thrusting his left fist forward, he punched through the Heaven Inquiry Blade and connected with Duan Hongchen’s face.

Duan Hongchen felt as if a mountain had knocked into him. The force was so immense that he had no way to withstand it. Any technique was rendered useless.

“The sea of suffering is boundless; turning back leads to the shore!” Lu Yang delivered successive strikes, each landing on Duan Hongchen, who felt as though all his bones were being taken apart. The latter was sent flying backward, and his vision darkened.

“Hmm? What is this?” The darkness before his eyes wasn’t because he was about to black out; something black was blocking his vision.

“Hair? Whose is it?” Duan Hongchen subconsciously touched his head.

So smooth... whose head is this?

“Where’s my hair?!” Duan Hongchen finally realized what was going on. Where did my carefully styled hair go?!

What’s the most important for a skilled cultivator? It is to act mysterious and unfathomable.

And the most integral factor is the hair!

With my hair gone, my air of mystery is half gone.

“Be careful, his Arhat Fist can make people lose their hair!” Duan Hongchen yelled to warn the crowd.

An Ke was originally planning a sneak attack, and her face instantly turned pale. Not seizing the Twin Lotus Flower is not a big deal; I can always find other ways to form my golden core. But losing my hair? That’s a big problem!

Run!

Without hesitation, she turned on her heels.

“Think you can run?” Lu Yang clearly didn’t have the habit of sparing his enemies, and he chased her relentlessly.

“Don’t come after me! I don’t want the Twin Lotus Flower anymore!” An Ke screamed, trying to show goodwill.

“You’re trying to make me let my guard down, aren’t you? I’ve grown tired of this trick!” Lu Yang thought from An Ke’s perspective and figured she was likely trying to deceive him just as he would.

Visit fгeewebɳoveɭ.cøm for the best novel reading experience.

“Don’t hurt Immortal Fairy An Ke!” Someone smitten by An Ke’s beauty attempted to block Lu Yang, only to be sent somersaulting in two punches, their hair falling to the ground.

“Stop, you thief!”

“Stop harming people!”

Many people tried to thwart Lu Yang, but they were all sent flying by his Arhat Fist.

“Can you give me a buzz cut?” someone asked Lu Yang softly.

Lu Yang nodded. He had practiced the Arhat Fist at the training grounds for four days, gaining the ability to customize hairstyles however he wished.

“Give me one!”

Lu Yang kindly sent the other party flying.

The entire area around the lake was thrown into mayhem. An Ke ran around the lake, while Lu Yang chased her. Anyone who came into contact with him would receive two punches and turn bald.

Fortunately, An Ke’s guardian protector appeared and whisked her away, preventing her from meeting the same fate.

“Come again!” Losing his target, Lu Yang soon found a new one.

Lu Yang’s Arhat Fist was as powerful as the original version, with the added effect of shaving heads. It was clearly a fist technique from a Buddhist sect. Even senior monks would compliment him as a “legitimate successor of Buddhist sects” if they saw it.

Regardless of whether they liked it or what their cultivation was, everyone received two punches from Lu Yang.

Lu Yang was like a lawnmower; not a single strand of hair remained in his wake.

“Let’s take care of this brat first!” Everyone was enraged. They decided to cease fighting over the Twin Lotus Flower and shifted their focus to Lu Yang, even ignoring Meng Jingzhou.

~~~

Beside the lake, the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes broke out in cold sweat upon witnessing the scene unfold before them. They desperately tried to make themselves invisible, fearing the crowd would vent their anger on them.

Heaven and Earth, please bear witness; we are just guides and have nothing else to do with Lu Yang.

“Excuse me, what happened here?” A gentle voice rang beside the ear of the hawk-nosed boss, startling the whole group. They thought someone had come knocking on their door to confront them.

Turning around, they saw a man and a woman, who had somehow arrived without them noticing.

The man was burly and looked like a barbarian, while the woman was slender and had a youthful face.

It was none other than Man Gu and Tao Yaoye.

Not long ago, Yun Zhi found Man Gu and Tao Yaoye. She told them that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had achieved considerable results with their training in the jungle and suggested they should learn from them. Thus, Man Gu and Tao Yaoye traveled by flying vessel and carriage, making several detours before finally arriving at the Demon Suppression Pass.

Upon reaching the Demon Suppression Pass, they heard that the Twin Lotus Flower was about to bloom, so they came to see what was happening and join in the excitement.

To their surprise, when they arrived at the scene, they saw a group of bald people fiercely fighting in the mud pit. It looked like a gathering of Buddhist sects.

Only after asking around did they learn that Lu Yang had used demon spells to shave people’s heads. His actions sparked widespread anger, and he was now besieged.

“Big Senior Sister wants us to learn from Brother Lu’s courage—unfazed by hardships and unwavering in the face of countless foes.” Man Gu was enlightened.

Chapter 254: The Fusion Battle Tactic Has No More Flaws!

“Fellow Daoists, may I ask if you know the two bald people in the mud pit?” Tao Yaoye asked the hook-nosed boss politely.

At the same time, she was also somewhat puzzled. I don’t remember Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou being bald. What kind of accident could have made them bald?

She fell silent for a moment. With these two around, it feels like nothing can surprise me.

The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes thought Tao Yaoye and Man Gu had come all this way for revenge, so they quickly shook their heads and denied knowing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“We just came too. We don’t know these two bald young heroes. But we heard that one of them is called Lu Yang. He seems to be from a Buddhist sect and adept at the Arhat Fist. Anyone hit by his Arhat Fist will lose their hair.”

Tao Yaoye, “...”

Since when did Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou become disciples of a Buddhist sect? Which Buddhist sect would be foolish enough to take in these two?

From what I know, the abbot of the Hanging Monastery is always clamoring about suppressing the Taciturn Daoist Priest, calling him a bastard.

Man Gu contemplated for a moment and understood the profound reasons behind their actions. “When we’re traveling outside, we need to conceal our identities. Brother Lu and Brother Meng know they attract too much attention and may implicate the Dao-Seeking Sect. Thus, they shaved their heads to show their resolve and pretended to be from a Buddhist sect!”

As expected of Big Senior Sister. She must have anticipated such a situation when she sent us to the Demon Suppression Pass to learn from Brother Lu and Brother Meng.

Sure enough, we’ve already learned a lot right upon seeing them.

“The two of you know them?” The hook-nosed boss noticed the unusual expressions on Tao Yaoye’s and Man Gu’s faces and suspected they knew one another.

“I’m Tao Yaoye, and this is Man Gu. The two in the mud pit are Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. We are all disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect,” Tao Yaoye explained.

“Dao-Seeking Sect?!” The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes were flabbergasted, not expecting Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to hail from such impressive backgrounds.

Upon further thought, it does make sense. These two young heroes effortlessly defeated the successor of a first-class sect, which means their backing must be far stronger than a first-class sect.

But learning that they’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect is truly intimidating.

What’s the Dao-Seeking Sect? It is one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, with a history of over 120,000 years, even longer than the Great Xia Dynasty! Their foundation is unfathomable, and there are rumors that the Dao-Seeking Sect is the leader of the Five Great Immortal Sects in terms of strength!

They’re the strongest sect!

The hook-nosed boss heaved a sigh of relief. As long as they aren’t enemies, it’s a good thing.

Chapter 256: Mother-Child River and Twins River

“Back when I was an overlord and ruled an entire planet, I could do as I wished and bestow blessings upon the world. This Twin Lotus Flower was a new species I cultivated.”

“Something like that happened?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy chattered nonstop in Lu Yang’s mental space. At first, Lu Yang treated it as background noise, letting her words go in one ear and out the other. But now, he was intrigued.

All this time, Lu Yang had a feeling that natural treasures had existed since ancient times, unchanged throughout the ages. For example, precious medicinal ingredients, such as ginseng and lingzhi[1], and other plants by the roadside, like green foxtail and wild chrysanthemum, had existed since the earliest records of humankind.

Since they were called “natural treasures,” they were naturally treasures nurtured by heaven and earth. Lu Yang had never heard of natural treasures being cultivated by formidable experts in later generations.

But now he had.

“Tell me, what’s the story?” Lu Yang asked eagerly.

“That happened after I became an immortal. As you know, I was incredibly renowned in the ancient era, and numerous people voluntarily worshipped me. “I figured that fulfilling such a wish wouldn’t cause any problems, so I decided to take care of it.” I’m an immortal with propriety; I don’t just grant any wish.

“Originally, I could have concocted a pill to help this believer conceive twins, but I remembered the Nine-Layers Immortal once said, ‘When one believer makes a wish, ten others will make the same wish.’ Childbearing has been a perennial wish throughout history; there are bound to be more than a few believers who wish for twins. Even if I craft a pill now, what should I do when others pray to me for the same wish? Continue concocting pills? That’s too troublesome.

“Thus, I came up with a solution once and for all—using my supreme mighty abilities to borrow spirit qi from heaven and earth, extract the Dao charm, and change part of the rules. Along with various methods beyond what you can fathom now, I refined a river into an immortal artifact. Anyone who drank from its water could conceive twins.”

“And I named the river as Twins River.”

Lu Yang fell silent briefly before asking, “...By any chance, you didn’t suddenly think of another idea and create a second river called the Mother-Child River after that, did you? Where any women who drank from it would become pregnant and only give birth to girls?”

“Since the ancient era has passed, I have no idea where the Mother-Child and Twins River went, whether they were refined into other immortal artifacts or hidden away by someone.”

The Twin Lotus Flower was a precious natural treasure that could aid one in forming a first-grade golden core. Lu Yang stared intently at the Twin Lotus Flower, hoping to form an offensive Yin-Yang Golden Core like his second senior brother did.

Tao Yaoye pondered adding yin and yang changes to her illusions to make them even more enigmatic. It would be ideal if she could merge these changes with her comprehension of Golden Core formation.

Man Gu stared fixedly at the Twin Lotus Flower, his mind filled with poetic descriptions of lotus flowers, such as “Emerging from the mire, unsullied by the filth; cleansed by water, yet never bewitching”[3] and “Boundless verdant lotus leaves extend to the sky, the sunlit flowers blush with a crimson hue.”[4]

Soon, another crucial question crossed Man Gu’s mind. “Can we eat the lotus flower? Can it be roasted?”

Just like that, the four sat in silence for two whole days.

Lu Yang studied the lotus until his eyes grew dry. He took out the eye drops Yun Zhi gave him. After applying a few drops, he felt much better.

“Did you comprehend anything?” he asked.

The other three shook their heads.

Despite two days of effort, they had come up empty-handed, which implied that their fortuitous opportunities did not lie with the Twin Lotus Flower; forcing the formation of a golden core wouldn’t work.

“It’d be a waste to just throw it away. We worked so hard to get it. How about selling it at the merchant guild? We can split the spirit stones evenly,” Tao Yaoye suggested. Trying to comprehend it further won’t yield any results, so we might as well give up now and cut our losses early.

“Sounds good.” Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu had no objections.

Lu Yang raised his hand with a different request. “I want the lotus seeds. I’ll just forfeit my share of the spirit stones from the auction. Would that be fine?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been making a ruckus in his mental space all this time, insisting on getting the lotus seeds. To appease the immortal and avoid calamity, Lu Yang had no choice but to claim the lotus seeds.

“It’s here!”

Lu Yang was bewildered. “Who?”

The two demon beasts didn’t respond.

The baby’s cries grew closer when suddenly, it stopped. An ancient aura burst forth, capable of causing everyone’s heart to palpitate.

“You’ve fought for so long and can’t handle even a few humans?” An icy voice rang in everyone’s ears.

Lu Yang reverted to his human form and drew his Qingfeng Sword in a defensive stance.

The owner of the voice slowly emerged, revealing its true form—nine serpent heads atop an enormous body that towered over ten meters tall.

Lu Yang exhaled slowly. “Nine-Infants Jiuying.”[2]

It was an ancient demon beast. From its appearance, it was clear that it did not descend from a branch lineage of ancient beasts like the tiger and lion demons.

This was a pure-blooded Nine-Infants Jiuying.

“You two, come and kill this sword-wielding human with me!” The Nine-Infants Jiuying commanded. "Although it had initially been drawn by the Ancient Barbarian bloodline, it immediately recognized Lu Yang as the strongest of the four upon arriving at the battlefield. To kill Man Gu, they would first need to eliminate Lu Yang.

The two demon beasts were aware of the Nine-Infants Jiuying’s petrifying abilities and dared not disobey.

Lu Yang asked, “Immortal Fairy, what is the opponent’s cultivation realm?”

“Advanced Golden Core Stage.”

A troubled expression came over Lu Yang. An Advanced Golden Core pure-blooded Nine-Infants Jiuying, along with two Intermediate Golden Core demon beasts...there’s no way I can defeat them with my current strength.

If the four of them wanted to, they could leave any time. Meng Jingzhou hadn’t purchased his Targeted Teleportation Talismans for nothing. The reason they hadn’t left yet was the tacit understanding between Meng Jingzhou and him—both recognized that this was a perfect training opportunity for Man Gu and Tao Yaoye. The enemy was right in the sweet spot of being either defeatable or undefeatable; it was a chance hard to come by.

Lu Yang cast a glance at Man Gu, who was currently engaged in battle with the armored demon beast, his Ancient Barbarian bloodline continuing to awaken. It was best not to interrupt this process.

Meanwhile, Meng Jingzhou and Tao Yaoye were occupied.

In that case, it’s up to me to deal with the Nine-Infants Jiuying.

“Hey hey hey, you can’t defeat it, right?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy expressed her concern for Lu Yang.

“I can win. I still have one move left. It works in theory, but I haven’t used it yet. I’ll need your help, Immortal Fairy.”

“Hmm?”

In the real world, Lu Yang slowly closed his eyes, as if he was falling asleep, his body swaying lazily.

All nine heads of the Jiuying sneered. “Sleeping Arhat Fist? That might work on me when you reach the Golden Core Stage.”

“No, this is not the Sleeping Arhat Fist. It is a fist technique I developed—the Lu-Style Animal Form Fist.”

“Lu-Style Animal Form Fist?” The Nine-Infants Jiuying subconsciously repeated.

With Lu Yang's movements, his body shrank, and his appearance gradually became more feminine.

“Empty threats!” One of the demon beasts scoffed and charged toward Lu Yang.

At lightning speed, Lu Yang’s soft fist slammed into the demon beast’s face, sending the demon beast hurtling through the air before it could even react.

The Nine-Infants Jiuying wore a grave expression as it glared fixedly at Lu Yang.

Lu Yang had completely transformed his appearance—he was now a petite yet peerlessly beautiful young girl.

“Lu-Style Family Fist: Huang Doudou Fist! Bring it on!”

The Lu-Style Animal Form Fist appeared to be a fist technique but was actually a spell that summoned a “god” to possess one’s body.

Lu Yang’s Animal Form Fist mimicked those he was more familiar with, such as the tiger demon he had fought, Meng Jingzhou, and Man Gu. Such transformation methods provided a small boost to Lu Yang’s combat strength.

Another target of Lu Yang’s mimicry was individuals far beyond his cultivation realm, such as Yun Zhi. Once he transformed into Yun Zhi, he could borrow her power and enhance his combat abilities holistically.

A major drawback of the second scenario was its uncontrollability.

Lu Yang had tried transforming into Yun Zhi, but the borrowed power exceeded his capacity and forced him to return to his original form. He speculated that if Yun Zhi lent him less power, he might be able to use it without issue.

But Lu Yang didn’t have the courage to suggest that to her.

Therefore, Lu Yang usually treated the Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist as the Big Senior Sister Summoning Technique. He was brooding over how he should develop his Animal Form Fist to borrow power from formidable individuals when he suddenly remembered that the most powerful immortal of the ancient era resided in his mental space.

If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy is willing to share a portion of her power, wouldn’t that make me stronger?

In the midst of this crisis, he consulted with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and immediately performed a set of the Huang Doudou Animal Form Fist.

It really works!

Lu Yang stretched himself, finding himself as light as a feather and as swift as lightning. Every part of his body seemed perfectly constructed, allowing him to unleash his power to the fullest potential. Moreover, after transforming, he felt that the strength he wielded had increased drastically, as if he had shed his mortal body and exchanged his bones, undergoing a complete rebirth.

“Why does it feel like my brain isn’t working as well?”

Lu Yang hesitated for a moment, feeling a change in his thought process, but he didn’t dwell on it. “Forget it, it doesn’t matter as long as I can get stronger.”

He raised his sword with his right hand, the gleaming tip aimed at the Nine-Infants Jiuying. A confident smile tugged at the corner of his mouth. “Have you decided how you’re going to die?”

“You’re courting death!” The Nine-Infants Jiuying was enraged. It had never been treated with such blatant disregard. Howling toward the sky, its infant-like wails pierced the air like waves crashing over each other.

“You two, attack together!” It ordered the two demon beasts.

They knew how terrifying the Nine-Infants Jiuying was; resistance would only lead to death. Not daring to disobey, they pounced toward Lu Yang.

Lu Yang maintained his composure, his gaze as tranquil as an ancient well.

He took half a step forward and contacted the ground with his toes, slowly tracing an arc. With a twist of his waist and a flick of his right hand, the Qingfeng Sword followed along, outlining an elegant semicircle.

“Slash.”

The heads of the two demon beasts flew five to six meters away, blood spraying forth as they died on the spot.

Slashing Word Mantra—decapitation in one sword strike.

Whoosh! One of the Nine-Infants Jiuying’s snake heads passed through the blood spurting from the demon beasts’ necks, making use of Lu Yang’s blind spot to bite him. The snake's head revealed its dagger-like fangs that dripped with venom. Just one drop could turn an entire small lake into a death zone.

Lu Yang grabbed the venomous fangs with his bare hands, unfazed by the poison.

The snake's head realized something was amiss and desperately twisted its neck to struggle free of Lu Yang’s grasp.

Lu Yang’s soft hands appeared weak and harmless, but in fact, they brimmed with a frightening immense power that an Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivator shouldn’t possess. He gripped the venomous fangs so tightly that the Nine-Infants Jiuying couldn’t break free.

Lu Yang pushed his arms outward, forcibly plucking the two fangs out, causing the snake's head to scream incessantly in pain. Seizing this opportunity, he pressed down on the snake's head and slammed his knee upward, and the snake's head exploded into smithereens.

While Lu Yang was focused on dealing with that one snake head, the other eight snake heads ambushed him from eight different directions. No matter how insane his methods are, he won’t be able to block the attacks from eight angles!

“Arhat Fist.”

Lu Yang struck several punches with a compassionate countenance like a Bodhisattva bemoaning the pitiful state of the world. Sounds of Buddhist scriptures echoed, displaying supreme authority.

The so-called eight-headed attacks posed no threat in the face of the Arhat Fist. Putting its hair loss effect aside, the Arhat Fist was one of the supreme fist techniques of Buddhist Sects.

After taking on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s appearance, Lu Yang felt like his comprehension of the Arhat Fist had deepened.

The Nine-Infants Jiuying seemed to have been struck by eight punches simultaneously and flew backward.

“Fire of Infant Transformation!” It tapped into its hidden trump card—the power of its bloodline. Activating its bloodline, it spewed toxic fire from its mouth.

In its wake, grass and trees withered, unable to regrow for a hundred years. The Fire of Infant Transformation contained deadly poison and was second only to true fire. To wield such a flame at the Golden Core Stage was a rare feat.

“Three Flavor True Fire.” Lu Yang fought fire with fire.

The two flames clashed, crackling loudly. In the blink of an eye, the Three Flavor True Fire overwhelmed the Fire of Infant Transformation, devouring it entirely.

“Impossible! That’s impossible!” The Nine-Infants Jiuying roared madly, unable to accept that it had been defeated by a mere human at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. “What kind of demonic sorcery is this?!”

“I’ve already told you, it’s the Huang Doudou Fist.” Seeing the Nine-Infants Jiuying flustered, Lu Yang flashed a smug smile.

Nearby, Meng Jingzhou watched the scene, sensing that something was off. “Why do I feel like Lu Yang is smiling like a dumbo? Am I imagining things?”

Lu Yang’s smile faded as he gathered his entire essence, qi, and consciousness into the Qingfeng Sword, slowly bringing it down in a strike.

“Break!”

The Nine-Infants Jiuying felt as though its body had been nailed to the ground, rendering it paralyzed. It watched helplessly as the Qingfeng Sword approached, the sword’s shadow reflected in the snake’s eyes.

With a swing of the sword, it resembled the setting sun, symbolizing the end of all things. The Nine-Infants Jiuying was split into two. Its Golden Core erupted, poisonous blood spilling across the ground.

Lu Yang was worried about the poisonous blood contaminating the jungle, so he used the Three Flavor True Fire again to sear the Nine-Infants Jiuying’s flesh, turning it into charcoal.

“Smells so good!” Lu Yang sniffed and drooled.

“Wait, no, the jiuying is poisonous! I can’t eat it!” Lu Yang quickly snapped out of it.

“Strange, why did I have such an unreliable thought just now?” That doesn’t feel like my usual thought process. He tried to ponder deeper but found it too troublesome and gave up.

“Aiya, Lu Yang, you’re wasting my body! If you had learned my yangsheng health-maintenance fist technique, you could have killed the jiuying in one punch. Why go through all this trouble?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hopped around in his mental space.

“Is that so?” Lu Yang found her logic reasonable, but something still felt wrong.

Chapter 264: Did She Still Have to Use the Play-Dead Technique After Becoming an Immortal?

After listening to Man Gu’s unfettered imagination, an image involuntarily surfaced in Lu Yang’s mind.

Under the night sky, everything is pitch-black and silent. In the desolate jungle, the only source of light is the campfire, crackling and popping, which only amplifies the deafening quietness of the jungle.

A disemboweled goat has its innards pulled out as it smears itself with strange herbs. It stands over the campfire, performing some unknown dance as if it was a ritual offering to a wicked god.

This is indeed an uncanny scene, beyond humans’ current appreciation of art.

She could see the shadow of her own acquaintances in Man Gu. “You know what, I have to admit that although the barbarians’ brains are all muscles and don’t work well, when it comes to food, they have plenty of ideas!

If we really encounter Nascent Soul demon beasts, even the Huang Doudou Fist may not be sufficient as a trump card. It just seems awry no matter how I think about it.

In the jungle, demon beasts were not the only sources of danger—humans were too.

When Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou spent the night with the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes, they were ambushed by humans. Fortunately, their opponents' cultivation was mediocre, and the duo swiftly dealt with them.

Chapter 265: New Yet Familiar Face

In the depths of the jungle, a few disheveled figures tottered toward the outskirts as fast as they could, blood streaming from their wounds profusely.

Heavy pants echoed throughout the air. “Damn it, didn’t they say that Golden Core demon beasts are highly independent and never act in groups? Why are there so many of them?” Song Hua complained as he ran.

“Who the hell knows? Is there any use in talking about this now? Just keep running!”

“It’s all your fault! We didn’t have time to buy new Targeted Teleportation Talismans after we ran out, yet you dragged everyone back into the jungle!”

“Who could have known we’d run into something like this? Ask these two bodyguards; have they ever encountered a group of Golden Core demon beasts acting together before?”

“Young masters, could you stop arguing for a moment? Our top priority now is to get to the outer edge of the jungle. Once we are out of danger, we can discuss whose fault it was.” The two bodyguards were drenched in sweat.

They already knew that these four young masters were difficult to serve. Last time, they had bumped into a Six-Tusked White Elephant at the Nascent Soul Stage. This time, they had provoked several Advanced Golden Core demon beasts for some reason.

What kind of luck is this?!

In all their years as bodyguards, they had never experienced such an absurd situation. One of their companions had already died under the claws of a demon beast pursuing them.

“Awoo—” Among the demon beasts was a one-eyed lone wolf, its gaze ferocious and bloodthirsty. It was precisely the one that had brutally bitten one of the bodyguards to death.

The one-eyed lone wolf’s paws were crimson. It moved at alarming speeds, looking like it was soaring through the sky on clouds. Releasing a howl, it accelerated again, charging toward Song Hua and the others.

“Damn it, it’s the Red Cloud Wolf, probably a former wolf king defeated and driven out by the new wolf king!” Song Hua cursed loudly.

Hearing Song Hua’s curses, the one-eyed lone wolf’s gaze turned even more frigid. Pushing off with its hind legs, it leaped high into the air, aiming to bite down on Song Hua’s neck.

Song Hua turned his head, his face turning pallid the moment he saw the wolf’s gaping maw widen before him.

Just as he thought death was inevitable, he heard the cries of a sword in his ears, short yet powerful, encompassing an inexplicable charm. Only a true master of the sword could deliver this strike.

A sword was thrust toward the one-eyed lone wolf, frightening it into turning to escape. However, whether the sword was too fast or the wolf’s reaction too slow, there was no way it could dodge. The wolf could only open its bloody maw wide and take the full brunt of the sword head-on.

The Qingfeng Sword clashed with the wolf’s fangs, producing an ear-splitting screech that caused everyone’s hair to stand on end.

The one-eyed lone wolf’s mouth was filled with blood, with only half of their sharp fangs remaining.

Lu Yang struck again, swinging his sword at the wolf.

At the same time, three other figures engaged with the three other demon beasts.

Song Hua and the others were stunned by the sudden appearance of their saviors. Do we help them, keep running, or stay here?

Before they could make a decision, the one-eyed wolf king’s head was sent flying, its demise set in stone.

Lu Yang withdrew his Qingfeng Sword, a few drops of wolf blood splattering onto his face.

“Watch out! There’s still one more in the sky!” Song Hua yelled.

At the Golden Core Stage, demon beasts were capable of flight. Song Hua and the others had initially planned to flee by taking to the air, but a demon bird had been circling above, ready to target anyone who tried to fly into the air.

The demon bird had noticed Lu Yang’s presence. With a flap of its wings, it transformed into a meteor-like shower of arrows as it dived straight toward him.

Lu Yang had already noticed the demon bird’s presence. Without even looking up, he casually raised his Qingfeng Sword, as if he was stretching sluggishly in the morning. Then, the demon bird impaled itself on the tip of his sword, its head pierced clean through.

“Are you alright?” Lu Yang asked with concern.

“All of you are...” Song Hua and the others were shocked. Lu Yang’s outward cultivation was only at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. But how could an Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivator slay the one-eyed lone wolf and demon bird by himself?

“Tch, you’re still faster than me.” Meng Jingzhou just finished off another demon beast, his fists covered in blood.

“Meng Jingzhou?” Song Hua’s eyes widened upon recognizing Meng Jingzhou.

“You are...Song Hua from the Song Family?” Meng Jingzhou was somewhat uncertain. The person before him was in a sorry state and covered in grime, looking like a refugee. He was a far cry from the Song Hua in his memories.

Although the Song Family couldn’t compare to the Meng Family, they were still a prominent and affluent clan in the capital. The last time Meng Jingzhou had seen Song Hua, the latter was singing and dancing on a flower boat, his dance outshining even the top courtesan.

“Yes, it’s me!” Song Hua hadn’t expected Meng Jingzhou to be among his rescuers. He had heard that Meng Jingzhou had been missing for a year. However, judging by the Meng Family’s unruffled attitude, he had his doubts about Meng Jingzhou’s disappearance.

“Young Master Song, care to explain? What infuriating thing did you do to anger so many Golden Core demon beasts into chasing you?” Meng Jingzhou asked lazily.

Song Hua wasn’t like Man Gu, who carried the Ancient Barbarian bloodline and inherently attracted enmity. While it is possible to provoke one or two Golden Core demon beasts, how could he have agitated five demon beasts at the same time?

Song Hua and the others could only smile bitterly. “We really have no idea what happened. We simply ventured a bit deeper than usual, thinking of killing a few more high-quality Golden Core demon beasts as proof of our efforts upon returning home.

Chapter 266: Herding Sky Grass

Two months of rigorous training had given the four of them a deeper understanding of the jungle.

Demon beasts at the Golden Core Stage and above generally possessed a strong sense of pride. Unless they were provoked by something like the Ancient Barbarian Bloodline, which incited the collective wrath of demon beasts, they wouldn’t act in groups.

“That’s indeed strange. In theory, my bloodline should exert a suppressing effect on demon beasts, but I didn’t feel that during the battle just now.” Man Gu recalled the peculiarity during his battle earlier. The Ancient Barbarian bloodline always had an overwhelming advantage against demon beasts. Since awakening his bloodline, Man Gu had never encountered such an unusual situation.

Lu Yang frowned, contemplating the reason.

“Ahhh, what is this?!” Suddenly, a piercing scream interrupted Lu Yang’s thoughts.

“Song Wuguo,[1] why the hell are you screaming?!” Song Hua chided his companion. Everyone was deep in thought, yet your sudden outburst threw all of us off track.

“L-look!” Song Wuguo sat on the ground, trembling as he pointed at the demon beast he had just disemboweled.

He had wanted to paunch it and extract the demon beast’s inner core as gratitude to Lu Yang and the other three for saving their lives, but the abnormality of the inner core had startled him.

Lu Yang walked over and saw that the lone wolf had been eviscerated. In its dantian area was a somewhat dim inner core wrapped in withered yellow leaves. The leaves were thin and densely packed, connected by white, thread-like strands that were sticky.

He covered his right arm with spirit energy and extricated the strange inner core. “There’s nothing odd with the inner core. Does that mean the issue lies with the leaves?

“Let’s dissect the other demon beasts!”

Everyone immediately set to work, slicing the demon beasts open. Soon, the results were clear—the inner cores of all five demon beasts were wrapped in the same withered yellow leaves.

Lu Yang racked his brain to rummage through everything he had learned, but nothing matched these leaves. “Does anyone recognize these leaves?”

Even the knowledgeable Meng Jingzhou shook his head.

Tao Yaoye and Man Gu also shook their heads.

As for those from the Song Family, it went without saying that their knowledge couldn't even compare to Tao Yaoye and Man Gu's, being limited to only identifying common spirit plants.

The two bodyguards, who had lived in the Demon Suppression Pass all these years, had also never seen such leaves.

“I keep feeling like I’ve seen this in a book somewhere... Could it be the Herding Sky Grass?” Song Wuguo muttered softly.

“Herding Sky Grass?” Everyone turned to look at Song Wuguo.

Song Wuguo immediately felt the immense pressure from their gazes. He was timid and had always preferred reading books to interacting with people. It was his first time being at the center of attention like this.

“Wuguo, do you recognize where these leaves come from?”

“It...it just looks familiar. I’m not entirely sure either, but I once saw an ancient text from the Great Yu Dynasty in the scripture library, and it was a notebook of a great pill-concocting master. It mentioned a spirit herb named the Herding Sky Grass, and the drawing in the book looked very similar to this.

“The book stated that the Herding Sky Grass initially grows like a weed. It possesses an impressive camouflage ability, mimicking the appearance of plants around it. When it is about to mature, it will begin to devour demon beasts, using them as nutrients to accelerate its growth. At the same time, it can also parasitize a part of itself within demon beasts, controlling their every move and making them go out to gather food for itself.

“The ‘herding’ in Herding Sky Grass is derived from its parasitic nature, meaning ‘to herd.’

“You know the corpse-driving spells, right? Legend has it that the cultivator who created such spells had drawn inspiration from the parasitic methods of the Herding Sky Grass.”

“What a wicked grass!” Meng Jingzhou furrowed his brow, sensing the malevolent nature within the Herding Sky Grass.

“Immortal Fairy, have you heard of the Herding Sky Grass?” Lu Yang secretly asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“There are a few minor inaccuracies, but it’s mostly correct.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s reply confirmed the existence of the Herding Sky Grass.

It was rare for Song Wuguo to feel valued, and he grew more excited as he spoke. “Big Brother Song Hua, this Herding Sky Grass is so rare that even Fusion experts may not have seen it. It’s incredibly beneficial for their cultivation. If we can retrieve it, bring it back to the family, and offer it to our great-grandfather, our status within the Song Family will be solidified!

“With some extra effort, the position of clan head might even be within your grasp!”

“Is this thing really so rare?!”

“Absolutely! That ancient text I read belonged to a Fusion pill-concocting master, and even he had only seen two Herding Sky Grass in his whole life. The records also noted that refining the Herding Sky Grass into the Herding Sky Pill can raise a Fusion cultivator’s cultivation by one minor realm!”

Song Hua’s eyes lit up. This is indeed good stuff. But he quickly regained his composure. “We almost got killed by the Herding Sky Grass. Given our abilities, how could we possibly pluck it and get out alive? It’s better to return and inform our uncles so that they can handle it.”

“But if we let our uncles intervene, how do we determine who gets the credit? Big Brother Song Hua, don’t worry, we actually have a chance to get our hands on the Herding Sky Grass.”

Therefore, neither the Meng Family nor the Dao-Seeking Sect will compete with us for the Herding Sky Grass!

Chapter 267: Nine Truths and One Lie—This Is Nothing More Than Child’s Play to Me

The five demon beasts manipulated by the Herding Sky Grass were no ordinary demon beasts. As Lu Yang put it, they were now at the Apex Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.

Given the improvement Tao Yaoye and Man Gu had witnessed, it went without saying for Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. With the headstart they had gained, they could no longer be assessed by the standards of the Foundation Establishment Stage.

These five Advanced Golden Core demon beasts posed no threat!

What on earth has this human done?!

Chapter 268: Premeditated

“The Epoch Immortal’s original form is the same as the Herding Sky Grass—a spirit plant that gained spirit sentience?” Lu Yang was shocked. A spirit plant developing spirit sentience is already rare enough, and even fewer have achieved any significant accomplishments.

From what he knew, there were two ways for spirit plants to develop spirit sentience. One was to live long enough to gradually gain intelligence, such as the little herb kings in the herb garden. These little herb kings had lived for at least a hundred thousand years. For a spirit herb to have survived that long without being harvested was a testament to its incredible luck.

Another scenario was when a spirit plant accumulated various coincidences, such as living in a premium-grade spirit stone vein for a long time, absorbing spirit qi day and night, or coming into contact with some principles of heaven and earth, attaining the favor of “Dao.” Alternatively, it could be enlightened by a formidable expert.

As spirit plants that developed spirit sentience were exceedingly rare, the world hardly knew anything about them. Even though the Dao-Seeking Sect had a few little herb kings in their herb garden, it was still difficult to study them extensively. The characteristics of each spirit plant varied greatly, and comparative research was challenging without a standard of reference.

However, one thing was certain: spirit plants with spirit sentience had abilities that grew tens or even hundreds of times more than those without intelligence.

For instance, the Herding Sky Grass before them controlled at least fifty to sixty Golden Core beings, and it was unknown if more were hidden in the shadows.

Once Lu Yang reaches the swamp, death is inevitable!

Chapter 270: Lu Yang’s Changes

Red silk in hand, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy appeared majestic and imposing. With a casual flick of her hand, she took down a Golden Core demon beast. Even her frown didn’t mar her beauty.

This was the first time Lu Yang had seen the Everlasting Immortal Fairy in action. Although she might have seemed nonchalant, that strike of hers concealed abstruse intricacies. From Lu Yang's perspective, her attack demonstrated her precise control over her strength, with not even a single ounce of it wasted.

It was important to note that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was using Lu Yang’s clone, which only possessed eighty percent of his power. If it were Lu Yang, he could also kill that Golden Core demon beast, but he wouldn’t have achieved the same level of finesse as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, wasting excessive energy instead.

Swish. The red silk was like a jiao dragon in the sea, sweeping away a Golden Core cultivator with every strike.

In just a moment of distraction, two Golden Core demon beasts and one Golden Core human cultivator had been cleaved by the red silk at the waist.

If a Golden Core cultivator attacked, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could control the red silk to protect herself; any hit that landed on the red silk left not even a trace. The red silk was at the same tier as the immortal treasures obtained by the Everlasting Creed. Even Fusion cultivators couldn’t scratch it, much less Golden Core cultivators.

“Who are you?!” The Herding Sky Grass demanded. It was startled by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s moves, overcome by an ominous foreboding.

I clearly saw Lu Yang use the clone technique, but why did the clone transform into a woman? Plus, this woman’s tone is outrageously haughty, totally different from Lu Yang’s demeanor.

Does this Lu Yang guy have a bipolar personality disorder, or is there some other reason? The Herding Sky Grass couldn’t figure it out for now.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sneered, not deigning to answer the Herding Sky Grass. “You’re just a sentient rotten weed controlling a horde of stinking corpse-like things—what right do you have to ask who I am?

“I can’t even remember how many things like you I’ve killed before becoming an immortal!”

Despite facing a bunch of Golden Core cultivators, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy showed no fear, as if she was accustomed to such situations.

Boom! Boom!

However, as the number of Golden Core cultivators joining the assault increased, the red silk’s movements became significantly restricted. It could no longer be swung freely to take down the enemies.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy immediately changed her fighting approach. She dropped the lushu horse, which was already reduced to mush, and twined the red silk around herself. “I see them!”

Chapter 271: Golden Core Formation

Lu Yang had entered an abstruse state. His perception of the outside world had significantly waned. He could only sense the Golden Core cultivators attacking him, while everything further away became blurred.

In contrast, the fog in his dantian grew thinner. It seemed all he needed was to part the fog to uncover the halo behind it.

A demon beast with the head of a tiger and the body of a jiao dragon lunged at Lu Yang. This was the hujiao tiger-dragon.[1] It was at the Golden Core Stage and an aquatic creature that could temporarily move on land. The Herding Sky Grass had specifically brought it out from the lake to hunt Lu Yang.

Detecting the hujiao tiger-dragon’s attack, Lu Yang exhaled a mouthful of Three Flavor True Fire, which adhered to the Qingfeng Sword. Just like that, the already sharp Qingfeng Sword was now enhanced by the Three Flavor True Fire, becoming even more formidable.

The hujiao tiger-dragon roared as it charged at Lu Yang. With a flick of his wrist, Lu Yang softly uttered, “Sever.”

The Qingfeng Sword sliced through, and the hujiao tiger-dragon’s head rolled to Lu Yang’s feet, the sundered area emitting a tantalizing barbeque aroma.

This was the “Severing Word Mantra.” While not as powerful as the “Breaking Word Mantra,” which drained most of his spirit energy, it could be used repeatedly and was slightly stronger than the “Slashing Word Mantra” against single targets.

The Herding Sky Grass attempted to control the hujiao tiger-dragon’s remains to attack, but Lu Yang had anticipated it. He activated the Severing Word Mantra once more, dismembering the hujiao tiger-dragon into pieces.

Another demon beast seized the opportunity to appear at Lu Yang’s feet. It was small and had three legs resembling a turtle. Holding sand in its mouth, it spat at Lu Yang’s shadow.

This was the yu turtle.[2] It could poison its enemies by spitting sand at their shadows.

With a backhanded thrust, Lu Yang pierced the yu turtle’s solid dark green shell, ending its life.

A bashe snake[3] and a feiyi snake[4] flanked Lu Yang. Both were serpentine ancient demon beasts. Striking at the same time, they planned to coil themselves around Lu Yang and strangle him to death.

Lu Yang used Draw Underground Prison to drag the bashe snake around, then shrank into the ground. The bashe snake didn’t have the chance to react before its dantian was shattered by the Arhat Fist.

The Herding Sky Grass felt that Lu Yang was growing stronger—his control over power became more refined, his movements became lighter and more fluid, and his combat style became increasingly ingenious, allowing him to achieve victory with minimal cost.

I must stop this change!

It shifted its focus from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to Lu Yang, directing more demon beasts to besiege him.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had also noticed Lu Yang’s changes, and a sliver of a smile involuntarily found its way to her lips.

As more and more demon beasts attacked Lu Yang, they were either slain by him or had their dantian shattered by the Arhat Fist.

In comparison, Lu Yang’s physical condition was worsening. The continuous use of sword mantras and Arhat Fist drained his spirit energy at an alarming rate; even the constant consumption of Great Rejuvenation Pills couldn’t keep up with the depletion. Several Golden Core cultivators had also inflicted serious injuries on Lu Yang. His left arm was fractured, and his abdomen and back were slashed multiple times, with the deepest wounds exposing his white bones.

Drenched in blood, he staggered as he walked. If this went on, he would soon collapse from exhaustion, fulfilling the Herding Sky Grass’ wish.

This was supposed to be a good thing, but the Herding Sky Grass couldn’t bring itself to feel happy about it. It had noticed that despite Lu Yang’s increasing number of wounds, his eyes shone as brightly as the moon, especially conspicuous in the dark jungle.

“Why are you smiling? Why are you smiling?!” The Herding Sky Grass bellowed, finding Lu Yang’s smile to be derisive and mocking it.

Indeed, Lu Yang was smiling, and he was smiling very widely.

“Why can’t I smile? A horde of Golden Core cultivators is swarming toward me, yet they can’t defeat an Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivator. Shouldn’t I be happy?

“Am I too strong, or are these Golden Core cultivators too weak?”

Lu Yang strode toward the Herding Sky Grass step by step. Despite his heavy injuries and nearly stumbling several times, he still sent shivers down the Herding Sky Grass’ roots.

The Herding Sky Grass frantically commanded the demon beasts to attack Lu Yang, without caring whether it could control them precisely. I’ll squash this human prodigy to death if I have to!

Lu Yang didn’t even have the strength to wield his sword and resorted to his bare fists to fend off the demon beasts, resolved to exhaust every last ounce of his energy.

At the same time, the fog in his dantian grew thinner. Or rather, it wasn’t that the fog was thinning but that it was absorbed by the halo behind it, making the halo more complete.

Lu Yang seemed to sense where the fog had originated from. “Is it the combat experience I’ve accumulated from challenging those beyond my level in the jungle?”

His body was undergoing subtle changes. The wounds on his abdomen and back gradually healed and scabbed over, and his broken left arm miraculously reattached itself. His essence, qi, and consciousness merged into one like a torch burning fiercely, with new fuel constantly added and causing the flame to flare even higher.

The fog completely dissipated, revealing the true form of the halo—a full and richly colored golden core.

This golden core was profoundly mystical. Its appearance symbolized unbeatability, and as it rotated slightly, it swept away Lu Yang’s exhaustion.

Lu Yang felt an endless stream of power gushing out, far beyond what a Foundation Establishment cultivator could possess. The impact of this force easily broke through the bottleneck of the Foundation Establishment Stage.

Golden Core Stage!

“Yazi beast,[5] kill it!”

A majestic demon beast stood out among the Golden Core cultivators. It was the demon beast, yazi. Born from the union of a dragon and a leopard, it had the body of a leopard and the head of a dragon. Holding a precious sword in its mouth, it glowered at Lu Yang.

This was a great demon comparable to the Nine-Infants Jiuying, one of the overlords of the jungle. But in front of the current Lu Yang, it was insignificant.

Lu Yang extended his index and middle fingers, pressing them together to form a fierce shadow of a sharp sword.

“Go.” The sharp sword shadow slashed down and then vanished.

The yazi dragon-leopard glared at Lu Yang. An extremely fine line of blood appeared on its head, stretching all the way to its tail.

Lu Yang blew gently, and the yazi dragon-leopard split in two and collapsed to both sides.

Just this sharp sword shadow alone surpassed the power of Lu Yang’s strongest Breaking Word Mantra.

“You’ve broken through to the Golden Core Stage!” The Herding Sky Grass stared at Lu Yang in disbelief. All the previous shocks combined paled in comparison to this moment. It had never heard of such a breakthrough method.

Lu Yang ignored the Herding Sky Grass’s astonishment; it no longer posed a threat. He was now studying his newly formed golden core.

“This golden core seems to contain many profundities I haven’t discovered. It’s also not recorded in ancient texts. In other words, this golden core is unique. How should I name it... I’ve got it! Let’s call it the Primordial Unity Golden Core!”

Just as Lu Yang finalized the name for his golden core, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s delighted voice rang in his ears.

“Isn’t this my Unbeatable Golden Core?!

“Lu Yang, you little hypocrite! You said you’d never form my golden core, but deep down, you still feel that my Unbeatable Golden Core is the most suitable for you!” Having dealt with the demon beasts around her, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy nudged Lu Yang with her elbow, winking at him with a beaming smile.

Lu Yang blurted out, “...What the heck?!”

His impression of Yun Zhi’s cultivation method could be described by another word—absurd.

Neither was of any reference value.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stretched lazily. After the clone body returned to the earth, her soul retreated to the mental space.

After working hard for so long, I deserve a nap as a reward.

Chapter 273: Tying Up Loose Ends

It was night. After Lu Yang had uprooted the Herding Sky Grass, the Golden Core cultivators were released from its control, laying quietly in the swamp. Occasionally, someone stumbled upon this place and witnessed the corpses strewn across the area. Fearing something sinister was lurking, they turned on their heels and fled.

A gray figure drifted down and took in the scene of carnage. Picking up the now-useless roots of the Herding Sky Grass, his eyebrows furrowed.

An inferno of rage blazed in his heart. Years of preparation have gone down the drain. I must get to the bottom of this.

Chapter 274: Getting Carried Away

Since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was sleeping soundly, Lu Yang felt bad about disturbing her, so he began to study the Unbeatable Golden Core by himself.

Lu Yang’s spirit energy reserve capacity was higher than his peers, thanks to the amount of tofu he ate. After forming his golden core, his spirit energy reserve underwent a dramatic transformation.

“My spirit energy reserve capacity has increased at least tenfold, and the rate at which I absorb external spirit qi has also risen. As long as I don’t use destructive moves like the ‘Slashing Word Mantra’ and ‘Breaking Word Mantra,’ I can maintain a balance between spirit energy consumption and absorption during normal battles. This means I can save a lot of money on Great Rejuvenation Pills in the future.”

During the battle with the Herding Sky Grass, he had gobbled up Great Rejuvenation pills like they cost nothing, leaving him only a pitiful few remaining. It still pained him to look back at it.

“Then there’s the improvement in physical attributes—strength, speed, and reflexes—all far surpassing what they were at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. Now, I can even hold my own against physique cultivators of the same level!” Lu Yang laughed, brimming with confidence.

His physical fitness had always been his weak point, unable to match physique cultivators like Meng Jingzhou, let alone Confucian cultivators like Man Gu.

At long last, he had filled this gap.

Lu Yang was immensely proud of himself. My golden core is the same as an immortal’s and is second only to the Harem Golden Core, ranking second among first-grade golden cores!

Since the Harem Golden Core concentrates the power of the harem on one person, it’s considered borrowing others’ power, so it cannot be counted as the ability of one person. Strictly speaking, the Harem Golden Core is formidable because of its strength in numbers. Individually, none of the golden cores can match the Unbeatable Golden Core.

My Unbeatable Golden Core is the true number one golden core in practice! According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, this is even stronger than Big Senior Sister’s golden core!

Lu Yang felt that he was unbeatable, imagining himself capable of defeating anyone.

To put it simply, he was getting carried away.

“My spiritual consciousness has also strengthened.” The most obvious manifestation was the change in his mental space. If it used to be like a small single room in a hotel, it was now like a spacious apartment with four bedrooms, two living rooms, and two bathrooms.

Lu Yang extended his spiritual consciousness, and the entire flying vessel was within its range, something that had been impossible before.

“I’ll test it when I get back. I just don’t know what other functions my golden core has.” Lu Yang couldn’t make much sense of it even after examining his golden core for half a day. “Forget it, I’ll ask the Immortal Fairy when she wakes up.”

The flying vessel made its way to the next stop without any mishap. The array cultivator sought help and finally managed to fix the array before the flying vessel took off again.

After stopping at several major cities, the flying vessel landed at the entrance of the Dao-Seeking Sect, and Lu Yang disembarked.

Just as he was about to enter his mental space to ask the Everlasting Immortal Fairy what was going on, he saw her lying in bed and sleeping soundly as she cuddled the Unbeatable Golden Core.

Lu Yang was exasperated and woke her up. “Immortal Fairy, could you not hug my golden core? I thought I’d lost it.”

Lu Yang nodded. “I remember it’s a martial Dao from the ancient era, right?”

You can’t win. Pick someone else.

Chapter 275: Functions of the Unbeatable Golden Core
