Chapter 279: A Conjecture That Overturns History

The old general’s duty was to guard the Everlasting Ruins and prevent outsiders from intruding. The only ones who entered were Yun Zhi and Lu Yang, as well as the immortal soul residing within Lu Yang.

Upon heading in, Lu Yang didn’t feel out of place. The Yanjiang Branch of the Everlasting Creed had a secret domain which was a spitting replica of the Everlasting Ruins, designed to foster a sense of belonging and strengthen their faith in the Everlasting Immortal.

Everything from the floating platforms and the ancient structures atop them felt familiar. The buildings had given way under the erosion of time, making it hard to imagine what they looked like before crumbling.

Yun Zhi snapped her fingers. The collapsed structures floated into the air, piecing themselves together to restore their original form, as if time had reversed.

Visit frёewebnoѵel.ƈo๓ for the best novel reading experience.

Though different from contemporary architectural styles, these buildings couldn’t be described as “archaic” by any means. Modern architecture had evolved over three hundred thousand years since the Great Qian Dynasty, changing with the times.

The ancient era spanned more than three hundred thousand years. Toward its end, art, language, and other aspects of civilization were already highly advanced, no less sophisticated than today. The only difference was in style.

The main bodies of the buildings were grand and imposing. Though its pavilions were arranged irregularly, it created a picturesque scene. Even the gates were inlaid with topaz, jasper, and pure gold, exuding an aura of magnificence.

Yun Zhi asked, “Senior, do you recognize these structures?”

It was just the three of them inside the ruins, so there was no need for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to hide herself, and she emerged from the mental space. She examined the buildings, then shook her head gently. “I don’t recognize these structures. Although I am clueless about architectural styles, I can’t help but feel that these don’t resemble the buildings from our era.”

A rare display of surprise streaked across Yun Zhi’s visage. “According to the Great Xia Dynasty’s assessment, these ruins date back 300,000 to 400,000 years. The Great Xia Dynasty has never made an error in dating. Moreover, the architectural style and layout here don’t match the early Great Qian Dynasty.

“The academic community generally believes that following the Ancient Nameless One refinement of the stars, the glorious ancient era, along with its countless treasures, was reduced to ashes. Hence, when the Great Qian Dynasty was newly established, they advocated for frugality and reduced taxes and rents. If we look at the buildings in these ruins, while they are not extravagant, they certainly have nothing to do with frugality.” This information was not from Yun Zhi but rather a report a group of senior scholars had submitted to the Xia Emperor after their site investigation.

“I don’t know then,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy admitted honestly. Pondering about such matters wasn’t her forte.

All this while, Lu Yang had kept silent. He hadn’t expected the exploration of the ruins to hit a snag right at the start, unable to determine even which era it belonged to.

Further ahead were the murals Lu Yang was familiar with.

In the mural, the androgynous Everlasting Immortal stood with arms outstretched, cradling countless planets in their embrace. On each planet knelt a small figure offering tributes to the Everlasting Immortal with their hands held up high.

Four months ago, Branch Leader Chu of Yanjiang Commandery had led Lu Yang’s trio into a secret domain. In front of a similar mural, he had explained the origins of the Everlasting Immortal, making them privy to the ancient secret of the Ancient Nameless One refining the stars.

So much has changed since then, Lu Yang lamented. It hasn’t even been that long. Branch Leader Chu was such a good person, yet he was gone just like that. But the culprit remains at large, unpunished to this day.

To the right of the mural was a long passage of text that Lu Yang couldn’t understand. “Is this the script from ancient times?”

Yun Zhi nodded, giving Lu Yang a rough translation. The text essentially stated that the Everlasting Immortal had protected humanity during the ancient era, fighting against the Ancient Nameless One and eventually dying of exhaustion. However, as long as the Everlasting Immortal’s name was uttered, they could be resurrected.

It was now confirmed that this segment of history was fabricated. Neither the Everlasting Immortal Fairy Huang Doudou nor the Everlasting Immortal Bu Yaolian had done such a thing. The former had perished before the Ancient Nameless One refined the stars, while the latter had only been born a few months ago.

“So these are actually ruins from the ancient era?” Lu Yang furrowed his brow. He couldn’t shake off the feeling that things weren’t so straightforward.

Yun Zhi shook her head. “In the past, I might have thought so. But after hearing what Senior has shared, I now suspect that the text on the mural was deliberately left by the mastermind to mislead us.”

She turned to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Senior, I’ve translated most of the text, but people in this era cannot fully decipher the ancient language. This signature is one example; neither the scholars sent by the court nor I can translate it.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stared at the signature and frowned. Of course, I can understand it, but this sentence is so strange that I thought I might be mistaken.

She enunciated every word. “May the Everlasting Immortal bless the Legacy Ember Dynasty to last for eternity.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy questioned, “What is the Legacy Ember Dynasty?”

Lu Yang was also bemused. He had never heard of a dynasty called “Legacy Ember.”

From a chronological perspective, after the ancient era ended, the Great Qian Dynasty was built upon the ruins. One hundred thousand years later, the Great Yu Dynasty replaced the Great Qian Dynasty. Another hundred thousand years passed, and the Great Xia Dynasty was born, continuing to this day.

There was no place for the “Legacy Ember Dynasty.” According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, this dynasty also couldn’t have existed during the ancient era.

Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked toward Yun Zhi, hoping for an answer.

Yun Zhi frowned slightly, equally perplexed. “I’ve never heard of the Legacy Ember Dynasty either. Could it be that this dynasty existed during ancient times?”

Lu Yang rejected the theory. “That’s impossible. The Immortal Fairy told me that there were only tribes during the ancient era. Even concepts like “dynasty” and “law” didn’t exist.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded in affirmation.

Lu Yang put forth a supposition. “Is it possible that after the Immortal Fairy perished, the notion of a dynasty emerged, and one was established?”

Yun Zhi shook her head. “After Senior perished, the Ancient Nameless One soon refined the continent, erasing everyone who knew the Immortal Fairy’s name. The time between these two events couldn’t have been long enough to establish a dynasty.” In other words, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s demise marked the beginning of the end of the ancient era.

Suddenly, a conjecture sprouted in Lu Yang’s mind, but it was so shocking that it could overturn the world’s understanding. “Since we have eliminated all other possibilities, only two remain.

“The first possibility is that the mural was created by a mastermind behind the scenes, who fabricated the nonexistent 'Legacy Ember Dynasty' as a red herring.

“The problem with the first possibility is that fabricating a nonexistent dynasty would be too easy to expose, making it pointless.

“The second possibility is that between the ancient era and the Great Qian Dynasty, there was another dynasty called the Legacy Ember Dynasty. This was supposed to be the true first dynasty in history. Furthermore, the Legacy Ember Dynasty’s legacy, language, and wealth were inherited from ancient times. It was only after the fall of the Legacy Ember Dynasty that the ancient legacy was completely severed.

“The problem with the possibility is—why doesn’t anyone know of the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s existence? How could the rise and fall of a dynasty leave not a single trace in the annals?”

Chapter 280: Worshipping the Everlasting Immortal Fairy

If the second possibility were true, it would be hard to imagine that something as significant as the rise and fall of a dynasty would go unrecorded.

In fact, not even its name remained, much less any records.

Who was the founding emperor? How long did the dynasty last? How many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators were there? What caused its downfall? Why was there not a single trace of its existence in the records? All of these questions couldn’t be answered.

The most critical question was the last one. Perhaps the method used was similar to how the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was erased.

“Immortal Fairy, when an immortal perishes, are there any celestial phenomena?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was caught off guard by the question. “There has never been a case of immortals perishing in history, so who would know if there will be any unusual phenomena...oh wait, I’ve died before.

“But I wouldn’t know what happened after I died either. There were probably no unusual celestial phenomena?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sounded uncertain.

“There were no unusual phenomena,” Yun Zhi answered on behalf of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, which surprised Lu Yang.

How does Big Senior Sister know that? Lu Yang didn’t dwell on this question. If an immortal’s demise doesn’t cause any unusual phenomena, it’s possible that no one even knows when an immortal has perished.

But why didn’t the four ancient immortals revive the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

Is it because they didn’t want to, were unable to, or simply because they weren’t aware that she had died?

Wait, even if they didn’t know about her demise, over the course of three hundred thousand years, they should have realized something happened to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and that she needed to be resurrected.

“Don’t think about this anymore,” Yun Zhi advised. She didn’t linger in front of the mural. She walked away, and Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy quickly followed.

“The only text in the ruins is on the mural. Since we can’t find an answer at this stage, let’s just think about it again after we’ve gathered sufficient information.” Yun Zhi reminded Lu Yang not to obsess over the question and trap himself in a blind alley.

Lu Yang nodded obediently and stopped thinking about the matter.

“There are nineteen floating platforms in this ruin. Although that’s a lot, the layouts of these structures are largely similar.”

Yun Zhi spread out her hand, constructing a model of the ruins in her palm. Eighteen floating platforms surrounded and protected the largest one in a regular arrangement, as if they were enacting some kind of ritualistic offering.

On the largest floating platform, numerous pavilions stood in a similar protective formation, guarding the central altar.

This altar was where the three were headed.

The more the Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at the layout, the more familiar it seemed. “This ritual setup...why does it look like how they worshipped me in ancient times?”

“Similar to how they worshipped you?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded and revealed another secret of the immortals. “That’s right. After I became an immortal, the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others forced a planet on me. They said that as an immortal, I needed followers to showcase my mighty power and the dignity of an immortal. I thought it was too much trouble, but they convinced me it was no big deal and that they could design a ritual process for me.

“The ritual method here is similar to what the other immortals had designed. They claimed that the number ‘eighteen’ has a special significance in cultivation. Nine represents the pinnacle, so eighteen represents double the pinnacle—the pinnacle of the pinnacle. This ritual symbolizes that I’ll receive eighteen types of empowerment, allowing me to last for eternity. It is the most exalted form of worship; not even the other four immortals carried out such a ritual.”

Lu Yang gasped. The Immortal Fairy truly commands a high status. Four immortals had gone out of their way to design a ritual process for her and even explained its design philosophy?!

The four ancient immortals were really magnanimous; they didn’t mind the Everlasting Immortal Fairy constantly stirring up trouble for them. Perhaps it’s only with such a mindset that they could become immortals.

Lu Yang was enlightened, but something still felt off.

Yun Zhi had been quietly listening to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s story, and she wore a peculiar expression. “But according to the research of the senior scholars and the ancient records, it is believed that this is an obscure array from the ancient era, called the ‘Eighteen Hells Devil-Slaying Array.’”[1]

Lu Yang felt that everything made sense now.

On the other hand, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy gritted her teeth, wishing she could challenge the four ancient immortals to show them who the strongest ancient immortal was. “Those scoundrels! I treated them well, yet they dared do this to me!”

In my opinion, they were already holding back. Naturally, Lu Yang didn’t dare to say it out loud in front of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, fearing he’d get beaten.

“I know! It must be because I beat them up too many times before they became immortals. Then, when they saw me form the Everlasting Dao Fruit, they were envious of my talent and tried to get back at me!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy soon identified the reason—she was too strong.

The three of them arrived at the center of the altar, where a hundred-meter-tall statue of an immortal stood. It was the same androgynous Everlasting Immortal statue Lu Yang had seen before. This appeared to be where the statue had originated. It was upon seeing this statue that the first creed leader founded the Everlasting Creed.

At the feet of the statue were various rare delicacies made from rare treasures, the most inferior of which were five-thousand-year-old lingzhi mushrooms. Perhaps due to the high quality of the ingredients, they still hadn’t spoiled or grown mold after such a long time.

Chapter 281: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Kitchen

Lu Yang couldn’t help but recall the immortal treasures the Everlasting Creed possessed.

Yellow Millet Dream Pillow.

Toothpicks.

Poisoned chopsticks.

Aged vinegar.

Bed sheets.

Plates.

It does seem like someone had stumbled into a kitchen and randomly taken a few items. That said, to be worthy of being called immortal treasures, their power must be formidable, but as for their origins...it’s complicated.

“As a chef, what I dislike the most is people entering the kitchen and disturbing me while I’m cooking. You understand that feeling, right?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked Lu Yang. As a barbecue master himself, he’s somewhat in the same profession as I am, so he should share the same sentiment.

Lu Yang actually wanted to say, “I’m just a roadside barbeque vendor—what kitchen do I have?” However, considering the unpredictable consequences of not going along with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, he could only go against his will and nod.

“Yes.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was elated that someone could empathize with her. She then sighed. “I never thought that someone would still manage to break in with the door closed. That shouldn’t have happened.”

“Immortal Fairy, aside from you, who can open this door?” Lu Yang suspected that it was the mastermind behind the scenes who had secretly opened the door, allowing the first Everlasting creed leader to take a few treasures and establish them as the creed’s prized enshrined relics.

“The four other immortals could. I was worried they might get impatient waiting for my cooking, so I told them the method to open the door. However, they were too polite. Not one of them came in.”

Yun Zhi shook her head subtly. It’s not difficult to break the seal set by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Given enough time, any immortal can figure out how to open it.

How strong can a kitchen’s seal be?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t do anything special. She simply stood in front of the door, and the mysterious symbols dispersed on their own. The door swung open, revealing the true immortal’s ruins—the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s kitchen.

This was likely the first immortal ruins ever unearthed, marking a momentous event in history.

As expected of the only immortal chef, the Immortal Fairy’s kitchen is speckless and bright, likely due to a dust-removal array.

After entering the kitchen, the door closed, cutting off the external light source. In its place, the Everlasting light illuminated the kitchen.

“It’s so quiet, as though it is completely isolated from the outside world.”

“Hehe, that’s all thanks to the soundproofing array I set up. When I prepare the ingredients, they often scream and make a fuss, disturbing the guests. As such, I set up soundproofing and spiritual consciousness-blocking arrays to prevent anyone outside from probing what’s happening inside.”

Lu Yang had an odd expression. Why does this sound more like a chamber for silencing people?

She reached unprecedented heights, earning the reverence of spirit chefs throughout history.

It’s a pity I died early; otherwise, I would have become the founding ancestor of spirit chefs and enjoyed being the object of worship.

When gathering with other immortals, I often brought up this story, specifically thanking the Nine-Layers Immortal for his support. When the other immortals learned of this, they would smile kindly at the Nine-Layers Immortal.

Lu Yang’s expression turned peculiar. “Did the Nine-Layers Immortal really say that?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy placed her hands on her hips and pouted. Her delicate eyebrows were knitted slightly, a sign of her dissatisfaction with Lu Yang’s skepticism. “When have I ever lied to you?

“A few days later, he came to me and asked me to cook for him again, wanting to take the meal with him. When I asked him why, he dodged the question and said something like, ‘The prisoner is tight-lipped. We’ve tried every kind of torture, but he just won’t confess. Looks like we’ll need some unconventional tactics.’”

Chapter 282: The Final Battle of the Four Ancient Immortals Before Their Ascension

“Did that prisoner confess?” Lu Yang blurted out.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was puzzled by the question. “How would I know whether the prisoner confessed? The Nine-Layers Immortal must have been too tired from interrogating and needed a meal to invigorate himself.

“Let’s see what ingredients we have left.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hummed a lighthearted tune as she wandered around the kitchen, eventually stopping before a pool of water.

“Taiyi[1] Holy Water?” Yun Zhi softly muttered, recognizing the origin of the water in the pool. It was no ordinary water but Taiyi Holy Water, so rare that it had never appeared in auctions.

Legend had it that the Taiyi Holy Water possessed the ability to purify all things and cleanse the soul. A single drop could pull a cultivator back from qi deviation. If Yun Zhi remembered correctly, only a few drops of Taiyi Holy Water remained in the world, scattered across various major factions as a prized treasure, not to be used lightly.

The Dao-Seeking Sect had once obtained three drops, all of which were used on elders who had fallen to qi deviation during their cultivation. Now, not a single drop of Taiyi Holy Water remained in the sect.

Yet, there was an entire pool of Taiyi Holy Water here.

The water’s surface was calm, reflecting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s delicate features.

“Why is there a pool here?” Lu Yang didn’t recognize Taiyi Holy Water and was simply baffled by the presence of a pool in the kitchen.

“It’s a pool for washing vegetables. Don’t you wash your ingredients before cooking?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy revealed an expression that screamed, “Lu Yang, you’re so unsanitary.”

Lu Yang’s eyelids couldn’t stop twitching.

Since the Taiyi Holy Water can purify all things, using it to wash vegetables is somewhat justifiable...right?

Yun Zhi was hesitant. As expected of an ancient immortal—quick-witted and able to blaze a new trail.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy lightly tapped the water’s surface with her index finger, causing ripples to spread across the calm water. The water’s surface seemed to have received some command, parting down the middle to reveal an underwater space.

The space below the water was free of water or moisture. A strange force separated the pool from the space below, as if the pool was the lid of a jar and the space underwater its contents.

What Lu Yang saw in the underwater space sent a wave of shock through Lu Yang’s heart. Unidentifiable beast meat brimming with vitality, immortal fruits long lost to the river of time, impossibly spherical stones, flowers shimmering with resplendent multicolored rays... Every item looks like they have an extraordinary story behind it.

But none of these is the main issue. The real question is—

“It’s been three hundred thousand years, and these things are still perfectly preserved?!” Lu Yang was floored. Even several generations of Transcendent Tribulation cultivators would have come and gone.

Yun Zhi raised an eyebrow. Based on her perception, time within this underwater space was completely frozen.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy ascertained that her treasures were intact and was secretly relieved. Then, she declared flauntingly, “This is a space the Epoch Immortal created for me! He used the power of his Epoch Dao Fruit to freeze time completely within this space. Whatever goes in stays exactly the same when it comes out!”

Lu Yang gasped. Freezing time in a localized space—the Epoch Dao Fruit could even achieve such a feat?!

“When the Epoch Immortal first ascended and formed his Dao Fruit, he couldn’t do something like this. It was with my help that he mastered this technique later. To thank me, he created this time-stopping space for me.”

“Immortal Fairy, you’re also well-versed in the power of Epoch?” Lu Yang recalled the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s time-related mighty abilities.

One is the Play-Dead Technique, which allows her to manipulate her own time, accelerating the decay of her corpse. The other is the “Weather Forecast,” which can accurately predict the weather.

No matter how I look at it, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy doesn’t seem capable of guiding the Epoch Immortal.

“The Epoch Immortal said that the power of the Dao Fruit could only be unleashed when facing a threat. But for an immortal, hardly anything could be considered a ‘threat.’ Thus, he asked me to cook for him. He wanted to freeze his own time while eating. After a few days of practice, he succeeded.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“While he was eating, he probably remembered the time I pinned him to the ground and beat him up when he was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, thereby triggering a sense of ‘threat.’ The Nine-Layers Immortal taught me that this is called a conditioned reflex.”

“Transcendent Tribulation Stage?” Yun Zhi was reminded of a story she had read in an ancient text. “Immortal Fairy, do you know about the grand battle the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the other three immortals underwent before they ascended to immortals, when they were still at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?”

“The final battle before ascending to immortals?” Lu Yang was instantly intrigued. This sounded like a tale full of drama, evoking all sorts of thrilling imaginations.

Yun Zhi nodded gently, recalling the contents of the ancient text. “It is said that before the four ancient immortals achieved their Dao, they engaged in a grand decisive battle.

So this is the truth behind the legendary final battle of the four ancient immortals before their ascension?

Lu Yang sneaked a glance at Yun Zhi’s reaction. Now you know the kind of ancient stories I listen to every day, right?

Chapter 283: Significant Gains

Lu Yang could confidently claim that his knowledge of ancient times was now on par with that of senior scholars who had spent their entire lives in this field. Moreover, unlike the scattered knowledge of these elderly scholars, what Lu Yang grasped was all related to ancient immortals—the knowledge that those scholars coveted.

Previously, Lu Yang knew nothing about the ancient era, so he accepted whatever the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said without question. However, for someone like Yun Zhi, she had her own unique understanding of the ancient era, so it was harder for her to accept the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s stories.

This is the advantage of ignorance.

Lu Yang stopped dwelling on the discrepancies between legend and truth. He was curious about the items stored in this underwater space. “What is this piece of beast meat that’s brimming with vitality?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rubbed her chin, trying her best to recall what this chunk of meat looked like when it was alive. “It’s the meat of a bifang crane[1]...no, it’s the meat of a faceless hundun beast...no, that’s not either, what was it again?”

“Immortal Fairy, you don’t remember what meat this is? How do you cook it then?” Lu Yang was flummoxed.

Although the Everlasting Immortal Fairy is from three hundred thousand years ago, from her perspective, it feels like she was killed three hundred thousand years ago, fell into a deep slumber, and then woke up only to be reprimanded by Big Senior Sister. Since then, she has stayed in my mental space for three months.

That is to say that it has only been three months since she last visited the kitchen. How could she have already forgotten what kind of beast meat this is?

“Why must I know what kind of meat this is?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy retorted, rendering Lu Yang speechless.

“Encounters are the work of fate, and so are meals. Whichever piece of meat I choose, it signifies that it is fated to be part of today’s meal.” Clearly, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had her own unique philosophy when it came to cooking.

“Then what about this fruit?” Lu Yang pointed to a particularly eye-catching fruit about the size of an apple. It was pure white, with three faint halos encircling it. The halos radiated a glow that sprinkled into the air. Due to the stagnation of time in this space, the light that should have dissipated remained suspended mid-air.

“Ah, this? It's the Eternal Immortal Fruit I grew.”

“Eternal Immortal Fruit? What is it for? Does it grant eternal life?” Lu Yang immediately felt that this immortal fruit was of extraordinary value.

Eternal life was the lifelong dream of countless people. Death was like a lamp being extinguished—no matter how powerful or influential one was in their life, they would be nothing but a mound of dirt after death. Everything from when they were alive would become useless.

If a single immortal fruit could grant eternal life, it would be a temptation even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators couldn’t resist.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded solemnly. Your guess is pretty close. “Whoever eats this fruit will have their corpse never decay—eternally everlasting.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Is this even remotely related to what I guessed?

“Senior, is this a Qingmu Immortal Fruit?” Yun Zhi pointed to another dark blue fruit, thinking it resembled the Qingmu Immortal Fruit that Jin Qinqin, a disciple from the newest cohort, had consumed.

A single Qingmu Immortal Fruit could give Jin Qinqin a constitution comparable to those with top-notch Dual Spirit Roots.

“Yes, this is the Qingmu Immortal Fruit the Epoch Immortal planted. I asked him for a few, and they tasted great. Now, this is the only one left.”

“And what is this stone? Is it a whetstone?” Lu Yang noticed a perfectly spherical stone and couldn’t understand why a stone was stored in a space meant for ingredients.

Even Yun Zhi had her brows knitted. She could sense a bizarre power contained within the stone, one that could rival that of a Void Refinement or Fusion cultivator. But she couldn’t identify what the stone was.

“This is a star core, the core of stars and planets. I dug it out from a huge uninhabited planet. You don’t recognize it? Oh, right, there are no more planets in the universe now.”

“So this is a star core.” Yun Zhi had seen it before in ancient texts. It was said to be an excellent material for refining artifacts, capable of producing immortal treasures.

But why is there a star core in the kitchen?

“What is this star core used for?”

“It’s an ingredient.”

Lu Yang was flabbergasted. “You can eat this?!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand, finding Lu Yang unknowledgeable. “What kind of question is that? If it weren’t edible, why would I keep it here?

“Don’t you know that the higher the energy content of an ingredient, the more delicious it will be? Star cores are top-tier ingredients in my eyes!

“Besides, isn’t one of the purposes of eating to replenish energy?

Lu Yang thought that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy made a few valid points. For an immortal, chewing a star core is probably as easy as nibbling a biscuit. But it still feels strange.

Could it be that I’ve always misunderstood the four ancient immortals? Did they spend their days happily munching on stones? Why does the image make them seem so...destitute?

“What about this flower? Is it also an ingredient?” Lu Yang pointed to a flower that emitted resplendent multicolored light and was frozen in time.

This multicolored flower was the embodiment of “color.”

As the three toured the kitchen, Lu Yang and Yun Zhi continually broadened their horizons.

Lu Yang thought, This kitchen totally matches the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s style.

Yun Zhi thought, With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy residing in Lu Yang’s mental space all this while, she won’t lead him astray, right?

I’m worried.

Seeing how reluctant the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was to leave the kitchen, Yun Zhi asked, “Immortal Fairy, you are reluctant to leave the kitchen?”

“Not really. It’s not every day that I get to see familiar things, so I feel a bit nostalgic.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy chuckled, somewhat embarrassed.

Yun Zhi nodded. “It’s fine. These things belong to you, after all. After we leave, I’ll ask the Xia Emperor to have your kitchen returned to you.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes lit up. “For real?”

“Yes.”

The three made another round of the Everlasting Ruins but found nothing new, so they departed. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy voluntarily returned to Lu Yang’s mental space.

The old general had been guarding the entrance to the ruins. Noticing the two emerge, he asked, “Did you gain anything from the ruins?”

“We gained a lot. I will report the situation regarding the ruins to His Majesty the Xia Emperor.” Yun Zhi’s voice was as calm as ever, unlike someone who had made a significant discovery.

“That's good then.” The old general saw them off.

Yun Zhi pondered for a bit. “I believe it was created by the mastermind behind the scenes. Let’s first suppose that the Ember Legacy Dynasty truly existed and that it worshipped the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. That would explain the origin of the nineteen floating stones in the ruins.

“As for Senior’s kitchen, I suspect that when the Ancient Nameless One refined the stars, Senior’s cave abode was shattered into several pieces, and the kitchen was one of them.

“The mastermind then refined the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s ritual site into the main body of the Everlasting Ruins and integrated Senior’s kitchen into the Everlasting Immortal’s statue. That way, the first creed leader would not only learn of the Everlasting Immortal and establish the Everlasting Creed, but also acquire immortal treasures from Senior’s kitchen with the mastermind’s covert assistance, ensuring the Everlasting Creed’s survival.”

It wasn’t until halfway through the journey that Lu Yang realized Yun Zhi had no intention of heading back to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Instead, she was taking him to Dayan Commandery.

“Big Senior Sister, do we really need to go to Dayan Commandery?”

Yun Zhi said without much emotion, “Shifu is locked in Dayan Commandery’s prison. No matter what, we ought to pay him a visit.”

Chapter 284: The Inseparable Bond Between the Taciturn Daoist Priest and Prison Cells

Chapter 285: I Agree to Sentence the Old Taciturn Scoundrel to the Death Penalty

Mo Danxin[1] was the current governor of Dayan Commandery. His fairness and impartiality earned him the nickname “Justice Mo.”[2] When faced with flattery and bribery from other local factions, he remained unmoved and sternly refused. He also treated mortals and cultivators equally, not giving special treatment to the latter.

Furthermore, at the Intermediate Divine Transfiguration Stage, he possessed the highest cultivation in Dayan Commandery. With the support of the nation’s fortune, no one could threaten his safety.

He also actively developed the tourism industry, creating a unique food culture in Dayan Commandery and attracting more visitors to spend money, thereby stimulating the local economy.

Under his governance, Dayan Commandery flourished.

However, he recently encountered two unexpected events that he felt were beyond his capabilities.

The first matter was the imperial court dispatching troops to be stationed at the waste mountain, reportedly due to the discovery of a diabolic creed’s stronghold. It was unclear whether this was related to the fallen Everlasting Creed or the other three diabolic creeds.

The army was led by Old General Lü, a Fusion cultivator who commanded immense respect in the military. With the old general stationed here, the commandery governor’s worries were allayed.

The second matter was that a heavyweight figure was imprisoned in Dayan Commandery’s jail. It was someone who was second only to the emperor in status, the sect leader of one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, the strongest cultivator below the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, the greatest swordsman of the era, and had enemies all over the world—the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

Fortunately, this big shot was cooperative. Once imprisoned, he would always stay in jail without resistance. If he really did resist, however, Mo Danxin wouldn’t have been able to keep him locked up.

From a legal standpoint, Mo Danxin had jurisdiction over the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s case. Moreover, his offense wasn’t serious, and a few days in prison would suffice. However, Mo Danxin felt that the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s status was too high and that the matter should be reported to the imperial court.

Furthermore, Mo Danxin faced another problem—the Taciturn Daoist Priest was indeed locked up, but he had started storytelling in prison, attracting many fans.

For instance, according to the law, someone who stole a few tales of silver would be imprisoned for five days. With family members delivering meals, the jail cells being warm in winter and cool in summer, and a Fusion expert telling stories next door, those five days in prison passed by in utmost comfort.

Somehow, word of this amazing experience spread, starting a trend. Now, the prison was overflowing with prisoners. To clueless outsiders, they might think that Dayan Commandery was a den of iniquity, with its jail packed to the brim.

If this snowballs into a rumor and reaches the emperor’s ears, all my achievements will go down the drain, and I won’t be able to salvage my tarnished reputation. I mean, who would believe that my prison is overcrowded just because people wanted to listen to a storyteller?

Fortunately, when the imperial court learned of this matter, they took it seriously. The Minister of Justice personally flew to Dayan Commandery to handle the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s case.

“Your Excellency, the Minister of Justice is almost here,” a subordinate whispered.

Mo Danxin hastily changed out of his casual clothes and donned his official robes before going out to receive his guest.

When he stepped out, the Minister of Justice happened to descend from the sky. Not a single servant accompanied him, which showed just how urgent this trip had been.

The Minister of Justice, Xu Xin, was tall and imposing, with sharp facial features, and his brocade robes highlighted his noble status. With his profound understanding of the law, he earned the trust of the Xia Emperor.

“Lord Xu, regarding the matter of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s leader...”

Xu Xin waved his hand. “I’m already aware of the situation. I agree to sentence that old Taciturn scoundrel to the death penalty!”

“Ah? But the leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect is...”

“Death penalty!” Xu Xin declared resolutely.

Seeing how firm Xu Xin’s attitude was, Mo Dan Xin was suddenly reminded of a rumor: it was said that if one randomly tossed a stone at the officials in the imperial capital, chances were it would strike someone who was an enemy of the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

There was even a poem: Who in the world does not know of you?

This referred to the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“Come on, let’s go see that old Taciturn scoundrel!” Xu Xin dragged Mo Danxin to the prison.

Upon hearing that the Taciturn Daoist Priest was imprisoned in Dayan Commandery, the Minister of Justice had stood his colleagues up and rushed over to watch the spectacle.

~~~

The jail was a hubbub of noise, as if it was filled with vicious criminals causing trouble.

But if one listened carefully, one would realize that someone was telling stories inside the prison.

“Let me tell you about that day when I and Qin Jiunian, First Elder of the Dao-Seeking Sect, were traveling the Central Continent. Using our Heavenly Eye, we discovered a tomb emitting a surge of corpse energy. With a quick calculation, I determined that a jiangshi king must have been born there!

Chapter 286: Even the Minister of Justice Is Not Spared From Imprisonment

The Taciturn Daoist Priest, whose real name was Ye Wanli, was 2,230 years old and currently held the position of Sect Leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect. During his time in prison, he attempted a jailbreak but chose to stop on his own accord. This was considered an abandonment of crime. He also voluntarily turned himself in, demonstrated remorse, and reported his accomplice. According to criminal law, he should be given a lighter or reduced punishment and could even be exempted from criminal penalties.

Xu Xin was 2,232 years old and currently held the position of Minister of Justice of the Great Xia Dynasty. During his supervision duties in Dayan Commandery, he openly discussed a jailbreak plan with the Taciturn Daoist Priest. He voluntarily opened the cell door and released the Taciturn Daoist Priest, knowingly breaking the law. His blatant disregard for the law and public act of assisting with a jailbreak caused a negative social impact, and he should be given a severe punishment.

Mo Danxin silently assessed the offenses of the Taciturn Daoist Priest and Minister of Justice.

As expected of the leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect. They have barely just met, and he has already sent a minister behind bars—and not just any minister, but the one most well-versed in law.

“Lord Xu, please step inside. I will schedule a trial to hear this case.”

From a jurisdictional standpoint, Mo Danxin had the authority to adjudicate this case.

Meanwhile, Xu Xin could be said to be the most proficient in law in the current dynasty, surpassing Mo Danxin in both legal theory and practice. However, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was too underhanded in his tactics, luring Xu Xin into opening the cell door. In his moment of impulsiveness, he had failed to see the malicious trap laid behind.

On any other ordinary day, if he released someone, no one would bat an eye. But it was different this time. With Mo Danxin’s obstinate insistence on following the rules to the letter, Xu Xin couldn’t seize the high ground.

Since I have no ground to stand on, I might as well spend some time in prison obediently. I’ll just treat it as a life experience.

Chapter 287: Ancestor of the Thieves Sect

“Lord Mo, what has my shifu done this time to end up in prison? Did he refuse to pay for services at a brothel, stage a fake accident on the street claiming someone knocked him over, or was he secretly selling Size At Will (Localized Version) again?”

“Big Senior Sister, when can we believe Shifu’s words?” Lu Yang asked curiously.

“When he’s not speaking.”

“And when can’t we believe Shifu’s words?”

“When he’s speaking.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Hearing what she said, Xu Xin slapped his thigh in delight. Yun Zhi’s words had enlightened him. No wonder it’s said that her cultivation is so high. Her ability to summarize things is not something I can hope to match.

If I hadn’t believed that old Taciturn scoundrel’s nonsense, couldn’t all of this have been avoided? Had I heard this summary earlier, I wouldn’t be sharing a cell with him right now.

Mo Danxin shook his head. “It’s none of those. According to our investigation, the Taciturn Daoist Priest has been in Dayan Commandery for over ten days. During this period, he has been well-behaved. He would then end each session with the phrase “please stay tuned for the next installment,” drawing collective groans from the audience. When night came, he would brainstorm how to continue the story for the next day. He’s been living quite comfortably.”

Lu Yang was dumbfounded. Shifu, so you’ve been making up all those stories on the spot?

Despite priding himself on his ability to fabricate stories, which was no less impressive than Meng Jingzhou’s, he acknowledged that even he couldn’t compete with the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s talent in concocting a story in one night and delivering it the next day.

“So Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect is your creation!” Xu Xin stared at the Taciturn Daoist Priest in astonishment.

Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect was widely popular; even teahouses in the imperial capital told these stories.

Xu Xin had listened to them when he visited the teahouses out of boredom. However, when he heard the tales of the Dao-Seeking Nine, which included numerous embellishments glorifying the Taciturn Daoist Priest, he was extremely displeased and stopped listening.

It was the same for other officials in the capital. They had listened out of curiosity, but stopped once they realized how far the stories deviated from their reality.

On the other hand, the civilians listened with great enthusiasm. Though the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s stories were exaggerated and fantastical, they were still tales of cultivators and a top-tier sect. The vivid descriptions of the cultivators’ actions and the colorful narratives captivated them.

“Do you have no shame? Aside from the name, is there any semblance between the you in the stories and the you in real life?” Xu Xin shot the Taciturn Daoist Priest a disdainful look.

“This is called appropriate embellishment,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest replied without a hint of shame.

Mo Danxin continued, “Just three days ago, during the monthly cultivators’ bazaar, the Taciturn Daoist Priest set up a small stall in a corner and sold a cultivation technique for enhancing movement speed, claiming that the ‘Ancestor of the Thieves Sect’ had practiced this very technique.

“When people realized they had been deceived, they confronted him and demanded refunds, but he flatly denied the accusations, insisting that his cultivation technique was genuine.

“Since the arguments led nowhere, the people came to file a complaint. Upon reviewing the case, I determined that the cultivation technique was fraudulent and decided to impose ten days of administrative detention.” freёnovelkiss.com

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had never heard of the title before. She tapped Lu Yang’s mental space to seek clarification. “Lu Yang, who is the Ancestor of the Thieves Sect?”

Lu Yang, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s golden finger cheat, proved to be as reliable as ever, ready to answer any of her questions. “Regarding the Ancestor of the Thieves Sect, I only know the gist of it. As you know, there are over three thousand unorthodox paths, and the Thieves Sect is one of them.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, signaling for Lu Yang to continue.

“There was once a legendary thief from the Thieves Sect. His unparalleled speed surpassed even his predecessors, and he was one leg ahead of the world. With him around, the Thieves Sect was completely redefined, making the Thieves Sect before and after he joined seem like different entities. Hence, the members of the Thieves Sect revered him as the Ancestor of the Thieves Sect, and the world commonly referred to him as the Thief Ancestor.

“The Thief Ancestor’s speed was so incredible that he could come and go from the imperial palace as he pleased, stealing numerous spirit stones and magical treasures. The most outrageous incident was when he stole the palace gates. The court was livid, but they could do nothing about him.”

“What happened to the Thief Ancestor in the end?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was excited. She had never faced a cultivator known for speed and was eager to engage one in battle to test her skills.

Lu Yang shook his head. “This is a mystery; no one knows what ultimately became of the Thief Ancestor. Some say he passed away in a seated posture, while others say he grew weary of worldly conflicts and retreated into an isolated life. There are also those who claim he failed in his attempt to ascend to an immortal and perished.”

Speaking of the Thief Ancestor, Lu Yang couldn’t help but be reminded of another figure, the second speedster after the Thief Ancestor—the Thief King.

The Thief King’s speed had reached heights where he was capable of going anywhere in the world. Thus, he defied the Thieves Sect’s ancestral teachings and stole from the Luodi Merchant Guild, subsequently vanishing without a trace.

In the real world, the Taciturn Daoist Priest continued to insist that he was falsely accused and declared earnestly, “It’s true! Practicing this cultivation technique I sold will absolutely allow you to match the Thief Ancestor’s unparalleled speed and be one leg ahead of the world!”

Yun Zhi fell silent for a moment, seeming to have recalled something. “Lord Mo, could I take a look at the cultivation technique my shifu was selling?”

“Of course, you can.” Mo Danxin summoned a subordinate and instructed him to retrieve the confiscated evidence from the yamen.

Not long after, the subordinate returned, panting and with a book in hand. The book was very thin and old; it didn’t even bear a title or an author’s name. It looked like those cultivation technique manuals that were stolen from a tomb and brought back into the light of day. It was no wonder that some cultivators were duped into purchasing it, given how convincing the book appeared.

Mo Danxin added, “The Taciturn Daoist Priest sold ten copies of this cultivation technique altogether. All ten of them were identical, and all of them were confiscated. This is one of them.”

Yun Zhi flipped to the first page, and Lu Yang also curiously leaned over to look.

The first page of the ancient book read: Those who wish to practice this technique should first sever one leg.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest threw up his hands. “See? I told you I wasn’t lying. Practice this technique, and I guarantee you’ll be like the Thief Ancestor in having one leg ahead of the world!”[1]

Lu Yang, “...”

Lord Mo, you certainly weren’t wrong to lock Shifu up!

And he still claims he’s falsely accused? Locking him up for a year or two wouldn’t even be enough!

Lu Yang began to understand why his master was the strongest below the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

If his cultivation was even a tad bit weaker, he would have been beaten to death long ago.

Yun Zhi’s expression turned peculiar. “The Thief Ancestor did only have one leg, which is why no one refuted his claim of being one leg ahead of the world.”

“Indeed, I’ve heard of this as well.” Xu Xin nodded.

There was one more thing Yun Zhi didn’t mention. When she flipped through the manual and performed some simple calculations, she realized that practicing this cultivation technique might actually allow one to achieve the fastest speed among their peers at the same cultivation stage.

So this is really the cultivation technique the Thief Ancestor practiced?

1. This was really hard to translate into English. Chapter 288: This May Be a Crude Dwelling, but My Virtue Makes It Fragrant

“That is to say, I made the wrong judgment?”

If Yun Zhi had been the only one who claimed that the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s goods were genuine, Mo Danxin might not have been convinced. But with Xu Xin’s corroboration, the credibility of the claim was significantly bolstered.

Lord Mo has already realized that his judgment was mistaken. I don’t need any compensation from the court. Just let me out.”

According to the laws of the dynasty, Mo Danxin represented the court. His erroneous judgment against the Taciturn Daoist Priest was tantamount to the court’s mistake, so the court was obligated to provide compensation.

Mo Danxin shook his head. “That still won’t do. You attempted a jailbreak earlier. Even though you didn’t follow through with it, you are still required to remain in prison.”

“Wait, hold on! I’m still not out!” the Taciturn Daoist Priest hurriedly called out to Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi cupped her fists and spoke with a hint of respect. “Shifu, as you often said, ‘A mountain’s height is not what only matters; mountains gain fame from the immortal they house. The water’s depth is not what only matters; waters gain spirit from the dragon they harbor. This may be a crude dwelling, but my virtue makes it fragrant.’[1] This prison cell may be crude, but with someone as noble and lofty as you, it won’t feel crude anymore.”

Hearing these familiar words, the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s memory was pulled back to several hundred years ago.

~~~

Back then, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had just taken Yun Zhi as his disciple, imparting his teachings at Heaven’s Gate Peak. The water’s depth is not what only matters; waters gain spirit from the dragon they harbor. You won’t find the little wooden hut crude, right?”

“Mmm!” Young Yun Zhi balled her hands into fists and nodded vigorously.

~~~

Now, my retribution has come.

Lu Yang nodded.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest, who had been fasting for days, couldn’t help but sniff the air. He recognized that the scent belonged to dishes from the best restaurant in Dayan Commandery.

Then, Lu Yang placed the food boxes in front of all the other cells. By the time he reached the Taciturn Daoist Priest, there was none left.

“What about mine?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest was dumbstruck. His mouth was still watering at the fragrance.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest, “...”

Well done!

~~~

Lu Yang had learned from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy that this cultivation technique was an extraordinary one.

Whoever could master this quarter would be accepted as his disciple.”

“He is living well.”

~~~

After Yun Zhi and Lu Yang left, Mo Danxin contemplated for a long time and felt that keeping the Minister of Justice locked up in prison wasn’t a good idea. It wasn’t that he feared offending Xu Xin, but rather that the Ministry of Justice had many matters requiring the Minister’s decision. “I remember there should be a legal provision for exemption from punishment... Found it.”

Mo Danxin flipped to a specific clause in the penal code, which listed six scenarios where criminal responsibility would not be pursued.

One of them essentially stated that criminal liability could be exempted should the Ministry of Justice interpret it as such.

Local authorities didn’t have the power to decide whether to pursue criminal responsibility; only the Ministry of Justice did.

Mo Danxin wrote down the details of the situation and had someone deliver them to the Ministry of Justice at top speed.

The second-in-command of the Ministry of Justice, the Vice Minister,[3] soon received an inquiry from Dayan Commandery. The Vice Minister of Justice snorted coldly. “I’ve heard that Mo Danxin is called ‘Justice Mo.’ But from what I have seen today, he’s nothing special. An official who knowingly violates the law should be punished even more severely. Exemption from criminal liability? Ridiculous!

The Vice Minister of Justice rubbed his eyes and cast three Heart-Cleansing Incantations on himself before reading the report from Dayan Commandery again. So I wasn’t dreaming?

“I heard that Lord Xu suddenly disappeared in the middle of a banquet yesterday. So it’s because he was in a hurry to go to prison?”

The Vice Minister of Justice wore an odd expression. According to the penal code, the approval of my superior, the Minister of Justice, is required to exempt someone from criminal responsibility.

Lord Xu would undoubtedly approve.

But the problem is that Lord Xu himself is involved in this case. According to the penal code, he needs to recuse himself and not make the decision.

Chapter 289: Meng Jingzhou’s Golden Core Formation

The life of the law lies in its enforcement; enforcing the law helped stabilize the national fortune of the Great Xia Dynasty.

Therefore, few dared to violate the laws of the Great Xia Dynasty, especially the criminal law, which imposed the harshest punishments. Although the law had to be strictly enforced, there were always unforeseen circumstances where the law demanded punishment, while common sense suggested otherwise.

In light of such cases, the penal code specifically granted the Ministry of Justice the authority to exempt individuals from prosecution, placing this power in the hands of the Minister of Justice.

In theory, this power could easily become a means for the imperial family and nobility to evade legal consequences.

In practice, however, such incidents rarely occurred, primarily due to the supervision of the Five Great Immortal Sects, which acted as a safeguard against the Minister of Justice acting recklessly.

But even the original lawmakers could never have anticipated a situation like this—the imprisonment of the Minister of Justice.

~~~

In the Mental Cultivation Hall, the Xia Emperor rubbed his temples in distress.

Why does it seem like whenever the Dao-Seeking Sect is involved, something new and bizarre happens?

He had received two pieces of news. The first was that Yun Zhi’s investigation in the Everlasting Ruins had yielded results, unearthing a non-existent Ember Legacy Dynasty. However, this wasn’t urgent; they could take their time to uncover more information about this dynasty.

As for Yun Zhi’s request to move the ancient immortal’s cave abode from the Everlasting Ruins to the Dao-Seeking Sect, he could agree to that.

The second piece of news was that the Minister of Justice was imprisoned in the same cell as the Taciturn Daoist Priest. novelbuddy.cσ๓

If the Minister of Justice dared to leave the prison, the Taciturn Daoist Priest would dare to spread the word that the Great Xia Dynasty was bending the law for personal favors.

If the Taciturn Daoist Priest dared to leave the prison, the Minister of Justice would stop him, ensuring he couldn’t escape.

A stalemate.

“Why don’t I pardon Xu Xin?” the Xia Emperor muttered to himself. As the emperor, he naturally had the authority to grant pardons.

After some thought, he abandoned the idea and issued another order.

“The entire Ministry of Justice is to relocate to Dayan Commandery.”

~~~

“So, is this why all of you have come to visit me in prison?” Xu Xin’s eyes bore into his subordinates, his expression so stormy it seemed he could devour them whole.

“His Majesty’s orders must be followed,” the Vice Minister of Justice said, struggling to keep a straight face.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest squatted just by the side. Normally, the Vice Minister of Justice and the others would have greeted him, but seeing Xu Xin’s livid expression, they didn’t dare to.

“Lord Xu, here are the official documents from the past two days for your review.” The Vice Minister of Justice respectfully handed over several reports that required Xu Xin’s attention.

Xu Xin snorted coldly. “Leave them here.”

Initially, the Vice Minister of Justice considered saying something like “Just wait a few days. Once His Majesty has had his fun, he’ll pardon you,” or “Do you need some food or bedding?” However, after some thought, he decided against it.

Only after his subordinates had left the prison did Xu Xin pick up the reports from the ground and begin reviewing them.

He frowned. “Nonsense! I gave it a lot of thought before proposing this system. Furthermore, it’s already been tested in select commanderies and counties and has proven effective. How could there be any errors?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest glanced at the contents of the report and roughly understood the situation. The report mentions that a certain system was useless and even increased the workload of the commanderies and counties, recommending that the rules of the system be streamlined. But this system is something Xu Xin took great pride in. How could he allow others to point out its flaws?

He chuckled, which sounded like mockery to Xu Xin. “Lord Xu, are you some kind of saint? Never make mistakes? If you’re so capable, why don’t you become the emperor?”

Xu Xin grew even more displeased, glaring coldly at the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Had it been Xu Xin’s subordinates, they would have been scared silent by now.

But the Taciturn Daoist Priest was not afraid of Xu Xin.

He’s my vanquished foe who has lost to me at the Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration stages.

With the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s vast knowledge and extensive experience in criminal activities, his grasp of legal theory was no less than Xu Xin’s.

“...Have you ever considered the legislative intent? Is this what the lawmakers originally intended...”

“...You’ve forgotten that the law has a lagging effect...”

“...Don’t give me theories. Is this how it works in reality...”

The debate between the two grew increasingly heated, with neither side willing to back down. They even set up a Soundproof Array to prevent other prisoners from overhearing their conversation.

In the end, Xu Xin’s tone softened, and his earlier sharpness faded. He couldn’t help but acknowledge that the Taciturn Daoist Priest made a few valid points.

“Shut up and let me think!”

Xu Xin lowered his head in thought. The old Taciturn scoundrel may lack morals, but he never jokes about such matters. If this is what he said, he meant it seriously.

This is exactly the result the Xia Emperor hoped for.

Although Xu Xin was devoted to the nation and worked tirelessly to fill legal loopholes, he would inevitably make some ill-advised decisions.

The Xia Emperor was helpless in this regard. Hardly anyone could match Xu Xin’s mastery of the Great Xia Dynasty’s laws, much less debate with him. It was challenging for the Xia Emperor to outrightly declare whether Xu Xin’s actions were right or wrong; he simply felt they were inappropriate. But as for how they could be improved, he had no idea.

Coincidentally, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was well-versed in the law and possessed a wealth of experience, making him the perfect candidate to engage in a debate with Xu Xin.

Hence, the Xia Emperor seized this opportunity to let the two argue it out.

Once Xu Xin realizes my intentions, he can be pardoned.

~~~

When Yun Zhi and Lu Yang returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect, they happened to run into Meng Jingzhou, who was just back from the jungle.

In the jungle, realization had dawned upon him, and he achieved supreme enlightenment, forming his golden core right after he returned to the Demon Suppression Pass. Leaving Tao Yaoye and Man Gu to continue searching for their own fortuitous opportunities, he made his way back to the Dao-Seeking Sect alone.

As for the minor incident on my way back, where I encountered a young master from an aristocratic family flaunting his wealth and humiliated him while in disguise, it’s not worth mentioning.

“Haha, bet you didn’t see this coming—this young master has also formed my golden core!” Meng Jingzhou began to boast the moment he saw Lu Yang. Though I don’t know what golden core Lu Yang has formed, I’m confident mine is the strongest; no one can beat me.

“Let me tell you, this young master’s golden core is unprecedented. I’m about to break the curse of the Single’s Spirit Root!” Meng Jingzhou was so full of mettle that he didn’t seem like someone who had just formed a golden core but rather someone who had just become a Transcendent Tribulation expert.

Lu Yang was genuinely surprised. “You have that kind of ability? What golden core did you form?”

Meng Jingzhou grinned, pulling Lu Yang into a teahouse. As they drank tea, he continued to show off. “I have a Single’s Spirit Root; as long as I want to, I can certainly form a Single’s Golden Core, right?”

“You’ve formed a Single’s Golden Core?”
