He gently knocked the teacups together, producing a crisp clinking sound of porcelain. Finally, he announced a conclusion he had derived after ruminating for a long time. “When two singles come together, doesn’t that make a pair?”

“So?”

“So, I formed two Single’s Golden Cores!”

Chapter 290: Equivalent Exchange Technique

Lu Yang leaned back slightly, as if he was startled by Meng Jingzhou’s golden core formation.

Two Single’s Golden Cores? Even the Cautious Solitary Daoist Priest wouldn’t dare to do something like this. This is truly a golden core or cores unprecedented in history.

He carefully chose his words. “Two Single’s Golden Cores... are you sure this won’t make you even more single?”

Meng Jingzhou waved his hand dismissively. “That’s because you don’t understand. As the saying goes, ‘When things reach an extreme, they turn in the opposite direction; when misfortune reaches its peak, only good fortune can come next.’ When something reaches an extreme, it shifts toward the other extreme. The same goes for my golden core. It has reached the limit of singleness, so it’s time for a change in the positive direction, like becoming popular with women. I already saw signs of this on my way back by flying vessel.”

“What happened?”

“While I was aboard the flying vessel, some local tyrant from who-knows-where flaunted his wealth and bullied the weak. I couldn’t stand it, so I casually revealed my identity as the eldest young master of the Meng Family. He got so frightened that he knelt and begged for mercy. Right after that, several decent-looking women gathered around me, drawn by my charisma.”

“...You’re really deep into this self-hypnosis, huh?”

Meng Jingzhou pretended he didn’t hear Lu Yang’s sarcastic remark. His eyes were shining, as if a bright future lay right before him. “In any case, I’ve already broken the curse of the Single’s Spirit Roots that plagued many generations before me. A new life awaits me!”

“Hmm? This little fellow’s golden core is quite interesting,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy happened to chime in, capturing Lu Yang’s attention.

“Immortal Fairy, what do you mean?” Don’t tell me this brat Meng Jingzhou has actually succeeded in breaking the curse of the Single’s Spirit Root?

“Have you heard of a certain curse spell?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked with an air of mystery.

Lu Yang shook his head. Aside from the Immortal Fairy placing a Tame Head Curse on the Ancient Barbarian Tribe, I haven’t heard of any curse spells.

“This type of spell may be called a curse, but it is actually a form of exchange, or rather, a rule. Some also call it the ‘Equivalent Exchange Technique.’ Using this technique, when you lose something, you gain something else in return.

“For example, Lu Yang, you are very smart, right? In that case, you can use the Equivalent Exchange Technique to lower your intelligence in exchange for unrivalled combat power!”

“So miraculous?!” Lu Yang was amazed.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was very pleased with Lu Yang’s reaction. “Hehe, now you see how knowledgeable I am. I bet no one in your era knows about this spell; you’re the first to learn about it!”

“Immortal Fairy, do you know how to use this technique?” Lu Yang developed a keen interest. If I could master it, wouldn’t I be able to exchange anything I want? I’d be unbeatable then!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head, dousing cold water on Lu Yang’s zealousness. “No one can learn this technique, or should I say, those who want to learn it will never be able to master it.”

Lu Yang was perplexed by this strange logic. If those who want to learn it can never master it, are you telling me that those who don’t want to learn it can?

“That’s right. Those who don’t want to learn this technique can master it.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “The ‘Equivalent Exchange Technique’ needs no learning. When a fortuitous opportunity arrives, it can be performed naturally. And those who have unleashed this technique often don’t realize they’ve already used it.

“This is just like the first person in human history to use a spell. He didn’t deliberately learn it or use it. Instead, it was a confluence of factors that the spell was unleashed in due course.”

“I see.” Lu Yang was visibly disappointed. I thought I could pick up yet another spell.

Then, Lu Yang realized something was amiss. The topic had drifted without him noticing. “Hold on, weren’t we discussing Meng Jingzhou’s golden cores? How did we end up talking about the Equivalent Exchange Technique?”

“We haven’t strayed from the topic. Previously, it wasn’t obvious, so it didn’t cross my mind. But now it’s clear—this little Meng fellow has already used the Equivalent Exchange Technique.”

“How so?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy analyzed it seriously, unraveling the secret of the Single’s Spirit Root. “Why is the Single’s Spirit Root so powerful? It’s because it trades one’s singleness as the price for tremendous cultivation talent and combat power. This is the true Equivalent Exchange Technique!

“If an ordinary Single’s Spirit Root cultivator were to have relations with a woman, the cost would be the loss of their pure yang body, and their cultivation would stagnate. However, with the reinforcement from two Single’s Golden Cores, if he were to have relations with a woman, his cultivation would plummet!

“This little Meng fellow has buffed the ‘single’ attribute of his spirit root, and with the courage to burn his boat to cut off any means of retreat, he has obtained supreme combat power in exchange. Among all Single’s Spirit Root cultivators in history, he’s probably the strongest!”

Lu Yang’s eyelid twitched. If Meng Jingzhou were to find out about this, he’d probably regret it so much that his intestines would turn green. Out of kindness, he asked, “Is there any way to resolve it?” fгeewebɳoveɭ.cøm

“Yes. The Equivalent Exchange Technique doesn’t apply to immortals. All this little Meng fellow needs to do is become an immortal.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Whether Meng Jingzhou can become an immortal is one thing, but even if he can, how many light years would it take for him to cultivate until that level?

Only five immortals emerged during the Ancient Great Era. And who knows how many more have appeared in the past three hundred thousand years? Big Senior Sister doesn’t want to tell me either.

Becoming an immortal is harder than climbing to the heavens.

Lu Yang mused, “That is to say, Meng Jingzhou traded the happiness of the lower half of his body for power in the latter half of his life?”

Respect.

“Umm, why are you looking at me like that?” Meng Jingzhou felt that Lu Yang’s gaze was peculiar. It’s hard to describe, but it looks like...pity?

He stretched lazily. “I just formed my golden cores, and I haven’t had my fill of battles in the jungle. I’ll go to the arena to exercise.”

After all, I have formed the unprecedented Double Single’s Golden Core; I gotta show off no matter what.

Before Lu Yang could react, Meng Jingzhou paid the bill and left, striding toward the lively martial stage nearby.

The fight on the battle stage had just ended, and the two combatants stepped down. Meng Jingzhou jumped onto the stage, radiant like the brilliant rays of a small sun. “Haha, I’ve just formed my golden core. Which senior brother or sister would like to come up and spar?”

I couldn’t beat my senior brothers and sisters when I was at the Foundation Establishment Stage. But now, we’re all at the Golden Core Stage. How could I lose?

“I’ll go.” A bald male disciple who seemed to have achieved minor success in his Buddhist Golden Body jumped onto the stage and flashed an honest smile. “Junior Brother Meng, please go easy on me.” His name was Zheng Jing. Despite his Advanced Golden Core cultivation, he wasn’t particularly outstanding among the other Golden Core senior male disciples.

“Haha, Senior Brother, please don’t hold back. I’m not the same as before.” Meng Jingzhou laughed heartily.

Before long, Lu Yang used a wooden clone to carry Meng Jingzhou down on a stretcher.

“You’re alive and well; why do you have to insist on courting death?” Lu Yang sighed, grateful for his Unbeatable Golden Core, which allowed him to know who he could beat and who he couldn’t. Otherwise, I’d wind up like Meng Jingzhou, being carried off the stage.

If Meng Jingzhou were still at the Foundation Establishment Stage, Zheng Jing wouldn’t have been so harsh. But now that Meng Jingzhou had formed his golden core and possessed enhanced resilience and recovery, Zheng Jing naturally didn’t pull his punches.

Just as Lu Yang was about to carry Meng Jingzhou back, three figures blocked his path.

He looked up and saw familiar faces—Chef Liu and Chef Gao from the barbeque shop.

“Please come with us.”

Chapter 291: You Two, Don’t Push Your Luck!

Meng Jingzhou stopped pretending to be sick and moaning, abruptly sitting up from the stretcher.

Chefs Liu and Gao were not clad in their oil-stained barbeque shop uniforms, nor did they wear the honest smiles they had when serving customers. Instead, they donned formal attire, their expressions solemn, as if they were reminiscing about the glorious days of the Everlasting Creed.

Under their gazes, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou felt a chill run down their spines.

“Please come with us. There’s something we’d like your help with.”

Chefs Liu and Gao had already investigated thoroughly. After Lu Yang and Yun Zhi returned, the latter left the Dao-Seeking Sect again for some reason, making this the perfect opportunity for them to make a move on Lu Yang.

If not now, then when?

But this place is too crowded. We’ll need to bring Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters—One More Time Barbeque Shop!

Previously, One More Time Barbeque Shop had been a small shop that had barely established its footing on the commercial street, surrounded by enemies and under the tiger-like watchful eyes of Fusion experts. It was truly a precarious situation.

But later, under the guidance of the creed leader and the Everlasting Immortal, and through the meticulous planning of the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups, the barbeque shop became a devil’s den of the Everlasting Creed.

As for the stealthy expansion of One More Time Barbeque Shop’s influence in the shopping district, the Dao-Seeking Sect remained completely in the dark...

“Let’s go then.” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou held their ground.

With two Fusion cultivators flanking them, they had no chance of resisting. Even if they were unwilling, they would be dragged along regardless. Rather than let that happen, it was better to go voluntarily.

“This way, please.” Chef Gao gestured, leading the two to the barbeque shop.

At the entrance of the barbeque shop, Lu Yang saw that the interior was pitch black, with only faint silhouettes of two figures swaying in the darkness.

When the two stepped into the shop, Chefs Liu and Gao stood quietly at the entrance like two iron statues guarding the place.

The moment they entered, Lu Yang felt like he was completely cut off from the outside world; he couldn’t hear any noises or see anything outside.

What he didn’t know was that aside from sounds and sight, the creed leader had also set up a World-Isolating array that blocked even one’s spiritual consciousness.

A light with no discernible source gradually illuminated the barbeque shop, revealing the appearances of the two dark figures—the creed leader and the Everlasting Immortal. Both were similarly dressed in formal attire, as if they had resolved to undertake something major.

“Please, have a seat.” The creed leader invited the duo to sit.

“Speak. What’s this about?” Lu Yang asked coldly, unsure of the creed leader’s intentions.

However, Lu Yang was not scared of him; the Everlasting Immortal was sitting just to the side.

As the ruler of the Everlasting Lineage, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had full control of the Everlasting Immortal, who was the source of the Everlasting Creed. With this connection in place, the creed leader wouldn’t be able to stir up any waves.

“It’s not something big. We just want to ask Fellow Daoist Lu Yang for a small favor. With your status in the Dao-Seeking Sect, it’s just a matter of a few words.

“Here, I heard that you two have recently formed your golden cores, so I have prepared some humble gifts. It’s a token of our goodwill. Please do us the favor.” The creed leader silently pushed two gift boxes toward Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

He opened the gift boxes, revealing their contents:

Exorbitant Foundation-Stabilizing Pills that could solidify one’s Golden Core cultivation. The remaining medicinal powder transformed into a base to aid future breakthroughs without leaving any residue or side effects that could hinder one’s progress.

A protective magical artifact capable of withstanding one full-force strike from a Fusion cultivator.

A book titled Cultivation Insights for Golden Core Cultivators.

Five small bottles containing materials related to the five elements—true fire, cleansed water, fertile soil, and more—usable for forging growth-type Five-Elements magical artifacts.

In addition, there were various other precious items—none of which an ordinary Golden Core cultivator could afford.

The two didn’t accept these “humble gifts.” Lu Yang went straight to the point. “Creed Leader, we’re old acquaintances. Let’s not beat around the bush.”

The creed leader slowly disclosed the plan they had been hatching for a long time. “Specifically, we want to recruit rogue cultivators, expand the scale of our operations, increase our influence on the Great Xia Dynasty, and make it such that the world cannot do without us!

“Once this is accomplished, we won’t shortchange you two; there will be additional generous gifts!

“You two may not know this yet, but our influence is secretly spreading. In fact, it has already extended throughout the entire commercial street, and the Dao-Seeking Sect is still oblivious to it.”

Lu Yang frowned. The creed leader’s words essentially imply that the entire commercial street is under their control. If we don’t agree, we might not be able to leave this street.

But he still didn’t relent. “What if we don’t help you with this small favor?”

“You’re not gonna help?” The creed leader slowly stood up like a mountain god awakening from a long slumber, exerting immense pressure on the two.

He narrowed his eyes at the two and threatened fiercely, “I’ve been very polite to you two. All we want is to open branches of our barbeque shop in the outside world. If you two push your luck, don’t blame me for kneeling and begging you!”

The creed leader felt that everything had been carried out to perfection. He had instructed Chefs Liu and Gao not to wear their staff uniforms but to dress formally and invite the two over with pleasant smiles.

Considering it was the sixth month and the height of summer, he had even specially reminded Chefs Gao and Liu to cast cooling spells when they met Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, so that the two wouldn’t feel hot.

Out of safety considerations and to prevent competitors from eavesdropping, he even set up a World-Isolating array to block any external probing.

He also cleaned the barbeque shop until it was spotless and free from grease.

The two protective magical artifacts were what he had crafted in all the spare time he had while managing the slaughterhouse.

The book Cultivation Insights for Golden Core Cultivators was personally written by the Everlasting Immortal, summarizing all the memories of the Everlasting Creed’s members.

The Five-Elements materials were purchased by him after visiting each shop owner on the commercial street and using every tactic to persuade them.

Opening a branch outside is just a matter of a few words. Yet these two people are still not satisfied?

The creed leader steeled his heart. A great man knows when to bow and submit and when to stand tall. For the sake of the barbeque shop’s ten-thousand-year grand plan, if worse comes to worst, I’ll just kneel! freewebnσvel.cѳm

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou quickly stopped the creed leader, utterly flummoxed by this turn of events. “You want to open branches of the barbeque shop?”

“That’s right.”

“Then what did you mean by recruiting rogue cultivators?”

“Recruiting staff.”

Since none of us can leave the Dao-Seeking Sect to open a branch outside, we have to recruit staff.

“Then what about expanding your scale of operations?”

“Operating the barbeque shop outside the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“And increasing your influence on the Great Xia Dynasty?”

“Become a major taxpayer.”

“And making it such that the world cannot do without you?”

“Getting more people to patronize our shop.”

Meng Jingzhou eyed the creed leader suspiciously. “You just said that your influence has secretly spread throughout the entire commercial street and that the Dao-Seeking Sect is still oblivious to it?”

“We’ve been underreporting our earnings to pay less management fees.”

The Everlasting Immortal added from the side, “There’s more to it. Our barbeque shop’s earnings in the Dao-Seeking Sect are already saturated, so we need branches outside to expand into new markets.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Why do you have to make opening barbeque shop branches this complicated?

Chapter 292: Second-In-Command and Third-In-Command

“You’re not just paying less management fees, right?” Lu Yang narrowed his eyes, recalling that Yun Zhi had demanded they pay the management fees and hand over all the remaining profits from the barbeque shop.

There’s a lot of room for manipulation here. For example, the barbeque shop could collaborate with other shops, with a portion of their earnings funneled into the barbeque shop. But Big Senior Sister doesn’t know about this. ƒгeeweɓn૦vel.com

Alternatively, they could use the barbeque shop’s profits to purchase assets, which wouldn’t need to be handed over to Big Senior Sister. When they need spirit stones, they can simply liquidate the assets.

It doesn’t take much for me to come up with seven or eight ways to circumvent the rules. I don’t believe the creed leader couldn’t think of them.

The creed leader’s forehead broke into a cold sweat, realizing he had slipped up by speaking carelessly.

“The two of you can take thirty percent of the barbeque shop’s profits.”

Lu Yang remained unmoved. “Hand over everything to Big Senior Sister. Not a single spirit stone less. You are already tiger-henchman ghosts and can’t cultivate. What use do you have for spirit stones?”

With Yun Zhi and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy backing him, Lu Yang didn’t lack anything. Yun Zhi would provide him with whatever he needed, and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had plenty of contribution points to spare, which she would give to Lu Yang if he asked.

I don’t need the profits from the barbeque shop.

Besides, even if all the barbeque shop’s profits are handed over to Big Senior Sister, she won’t manage the accounts. Doesn’t that mean they’ll eventually end up in my hands?

Meng Jingzhou went without saying; as the eldest young master of the Meng Family, his only worry was having too much money.

“If you don’t agree to these terms, I’ll immediately report the matter of you hiding a stash of spirit stones to Big Senior Sister. Feel free to guess how she’ll react when she finds out.”

More beads of cold sweat trickled down the creed leader’s face. As tiger-henchman ghosts, it’s true that we don’t have much use for spirit stones. Accumulating them is just to give ourselves a goal.

But the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Big Senior Sister may not accept this explanation.

Lu Yang said leisurely, “On the other hand, if you agree to these terms and fix the gaps, this matter can be swept under the rug. Big Senior Sister won’t find out, and I’ll also persuade her to let you open branches outside.”

“What do you say? Why don’t you think it over?”

The creed leader fell silent, contemplating the feasibility of Lu Yang’s proposal. Tiger-henchman ghosts are a type of ghost soul. Without a goal or spiritual anchor, we would exist aimlessly until our consciousness dissipates and we return to the heavens and earth.

As higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed, our spiritual anchor is the Everlasting Immortal. Since the Everlasting Immortal has asked us to expand the barbeque shop to the outside world and expand it across the Central Continent, we must fulfill his directive.

The creed leader cast a surreptitious glance at the Everlasting Immortal and saw him give an almost imperceptible nod. After a moment of internal struggle, he gritted his teeth and made up his mind. “Fine, I agree to your terms!”

“That’s more like it.

“By the way, do you know Qin Haoran, the Creed Leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?” Lu Yang suddenly remembered that the person before him wasn’t just a butcher from the slaughterhouse—he was also the Creed Leader of the Everlasting Creed.

“Qin Haoran?” The creed leader was momentarily stunned. “The previous leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed was surnamed Qin, but I don’t know his full name.”

Meng Jingzhou was puzzled. “As fellow diabolic creed leaders, how could you not know his name?”

The creed leader explained helplessly. “It’s true. The relationships between the Four Great Diabolic Creeds aren’t as close as you might think. We typically only meet and interact during joint operations or sparring sessions. Moreover, conflicts between our creeds’ core doctrines make it difficult for us to be united on the same front.

“For instance, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed believes in reincarnation, that people go to the Nine Netherworlds after death. In contrast, our Everlasting Creed worships the Everlasting Immortal, believing that the Everlasting Immortal can be resurrected. Our doctrines are vastly different.

“And it’s not just a matter of belonging to different creeds. Even within the same creed, we may not know much about one another.

“Let’s assume that Creed Leader Qin had a wife and children. Would he tell his subordinates? Of course not.”

Lu Yang nodded. That makes sense. If the Nine-Netherworlds Creed knew of Su Yiren’s existence, how could there have been no movement from them over the past decade?

Su Yiren’s existence is a threat to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. She doesn’t know about Qin Haoran’s identity or the location of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, but would the Nine-Netherworlds Creed believe that?

It’s more likely that Qin Haoran had deliberately concealed Su Yiren’s existence.

The creed leader continued, “However, I do know a bit about Creed Leader Qin. Under the premise of no immortal treasures, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s overall strength is slightly greater than ours. In fact, Creed Leader Qin once complained to me in private that he was under a lot of pressure, so I suspect his position as creed leader wasn’t as stable as mine, with many people below him vying for power.

“The Nine-Netherworlds Creed doesn’t worship an immortal, so they probably don’t have any immortal treasures.” The creed leader spoke with pride.

Among the Four Great Diabolic Creeds, we are the only ones who worship an immortal and possess immortal treasures. It’s a pity that we couldn’t acquire those immortal treasures in the Everlasting Ruins; otherwise, the Everlasting Creed’s strength could have ranked first among the four!

“The Nine-Netherworlds Creed believes in the existence of the Nine-Netherworlds, the place people go after death, so they’re not afraid of anything. They have proposed numerous radical plans, such as building a city at the entrance of the Nine Netherworlds and declaring war on the Great Xia Dynasty. But all of these were suppressed by Creed Leader Qin.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou gasped. They dared to propose plans like declaring war on the Great Xia Dynasty? Were they sure there weren’t spies within the higher-ups of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed trying to wipe them out?

If I use myself as an analogy, it would be equivalent to me, the creed founder of the Everlasting Creed, declaring war on Big Senior Sister.

I must have been possessed by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The creed leader continued to share more information regarding the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, allowing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to gain valuable insights.

After they finished listening to the intelligence, the two reckoned there was no need to stay any longer and got up to leave.

“Let me see you off,” the creed leader said courteously, escorting Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou out.

“Lu Yang, I have something to discuss with the Everlasting Immortal. I’ll be right back,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said.

“Alright.”

A figure slowly drifted out from behind Lu Yang. It was a beautiful woman in a pale yellow dress. She silently appeared before the Everlasting Immortal, who felt immense pressure as if he had reached the end of his path.

The Everlasting Dao Fruit was a superior existence to the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit, so the latter had no way of resisting.

“Immortal Fairy,” the Everlasting Immortal greeted with his hands crossed above his head.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy uttered a soft affirmative. “Since we have the chance to meet today, there’s something I need to inform you about.”

“Please go ahead.”

“I’ve observed that Lu Yang’s temperament and talent meet my requirements, so I have decided that Lu Yang will be the second-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage, and you will be the third-in-command. From now on, you must treat Lu Yang with the same respect as you would treat me. Do you understand?”

The Everlasting Immortal was surprised. Even if Lu Yang’s temperament and talent are sufficient, his cultivation realm is still low. How could he qualify as the second-in-command? But then, he seemed to have understood something and deferentially replied, “Yes.”

Soon, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy returned to Lu Yang’s mental space.

“Immortal Fairy, what did you do?”

“Not telling you.”

She secretly giggled. Lu Yang, you don’t want to be the second-in-command? In that case, I’ll make everyone believe you are. By then, even if you deny it, it’ll be useless.

I’m so clever.

Chapter 293: Li Haoran’s Pain

At the dining hall on Artifact Refinement Peak, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou found Zhou Lulu, who was reading a book while painting tangren sugar art.[1]

“Senior Sister Zhou, is Junior Brother Li on the mountain?” Lu Yang asked politely.

“Oh, it’s Junior Brother Lu and Junior Brother Meng. You have formed your golden cores? That’s fast.” Zhou Lulu looked up, a trace of surprise flashing past her eyes upon noticing the cultivation realms of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

At their age, I was still at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.

“You’re looking for Junior Brother Li? He’s in his cave abode.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou flashed a smile simultaneously. Since we are as close as brothers with Li Haoran, we naturally have to show off in front of him now that we have formed our golden cores.

Otherwise, what is the point of working so hard to cultivate?

“Junior Brother Li should be sleeping.”

“Sleeping? I don’t remember Junior Brother Li as someone who likes to sleep.”

“He wasn’t in the past, but ever since he returned from visiting his family, he’s started sleeping a lot. Every time he wakes up, he looks gloomy, as if he’s had a nightmare. I asked him if he dreamed of something bad, but he wasn’t willing to tell me.

“I asked my father, and he told me not to meddle in this.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged a glance, roughly guessing the situation—Li Haoran was likely dreaming of memories from his past life.

Qin Haoran was a bona fide diabolic creed leader who had committed heinous deeds. Coupled with what the Everlasting Creed’s leader had mentioned about many people coveting Qin Haoran’s position, all of this would make Li Haoran uneasy.

The two put aside their intention to show off and decided to visit Li Haoran.

However, it wouldn’t be appropriate to go empty-handed. Seeing that Zhou Lulu’s tangren sugar art looked quite fun, Lu Yang thought about buying one for Li Haoran.

Before he could ask, however, Zhou Lulu gently blew, and the two tangren figurines seemed to have come to life. Wielding weapons made of sugary syrup, they clashed in mid-air, creating clanking sounds.

The corner of Lu Yang’s eyes twitched as he witnessed this scene. If I’m not mistaken, these two tangren figurines possess combat power equivalent to the Golden Core Stage.

If I buy these two tangren figurines for Li Haoran, they might beat him up.

Forget it, I’ll find another gift.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou walked around the dining hall. There were youtiao that could grow or shrink to serve as roof beams, baozi that could be used as covert weapons, shaobing that could act as a Heart-Protecting Mirror[2] or chest armor plate, and fried sesame seeds that could be used for practicing Iron Sand Palm[3]—none of these could be used as gifts.

“The cooking standards in your dining hall are impressive!” The sole spirit chef gave the Artifact Refinement Peak’s dining hall a positive appraisal.

“I’d rather their standards be lower.”

“You’re so unambitious!”

Lu Yang pretended he heard nothing.

~~~

In a pitch-black cave, a person’s face was twisted in agony, his body involuntarily writhing, as if he was experiencing pain in his dreams. Yet, he was unable to wake up and could only endure the suffering in silence.

Suddenly, he opened his eyes, his clothes and bedding drenched in sweat.

The candlelight flickered, illuminating the entire cave abode and also Li Haoran’s face.

He looked around the cave abode in confusion, only then realizing he had woken up.

Recalling the experiences in his dreams, including the dark side of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and the unknown pressures Qin Haoran faced, Li Haoran couldn’t help but shudder and curse under his breath, “Damn these past-life memories...”

As for the occasional emergence of his past-life memories, even his shifu, Fifth Elder, who managed the Artifact Refining Peak, couldn’t offer a decent solution.

Li Haoran silently recited, casting a Garment-Cleansing Incantation on his clothes, then a Body-Cleansing Incantation. Only then did he feel somewhat better.

“Hmm? Senior Brother Lu and Senior Brother Meng are at the entrance?” The cave abode’s array alerted him, lifting his spirits.

Opening the door, he saw Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, both wearing bright smiles.

“Junior Brother Li, you’re awake?” Lu Yang smiled, subtly observing Li Haoran’s condition.

Li Haoran had dark circles under his eyes, and his eyelids drooped, making him appear dispirited. Ruling out the possibility of self-inflicted vitality exhaustion, Lu Yang could only attribute the cause to Qin Haoran’s memories.

“Please, come in,” Li Haoran greeted them warmly.

The two entered Li Haoran’s cave abode and saw sundry displays of refined magical artifacts, including armor, shields, and bronze cauldrons. If a Golden Core artifact-refining master were here, they would marvel at the extraordinary craftsmanship.

Li Haoran curled his finger slightly, and the teapot on the table began to move on its own. It grew arms and legs, clattering across the table. Then, it filled itself with water, added tea leaves, put on the lid, and sat on the stove to heat itself up. In no time, the tea was bubbling. The teapot tilted its body and poured tea into the cups, pushing them in front of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

The two instinctively said “thank you,” only to realize afterward that the teapot was just a magical artifact without sentience. Why were we thanking it?

“Junior Brother Li, I heard you haven’t been resting well lately?”

At the mention of this topic, Li Haoran slumped, a sliver of a bitter smile appearing on his visage. “You guessed it right, Senior Brother Lu. I can’t tell anyone else about being Qin Haoran’s reincarnation, so I can only vent to you two.”

Lu Yang patted Li Haoran’s shoulder, his expression one of understanding. “You must have seen many secrets of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed in your dreams, and these secrets have caused you boundless pain.”

Li Haoran nodded, emotional about finally feeling understood. “Yes, every time I close my eyes, all I see are the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s financial deficits!

“Wages for the creed members, expenses for handling aftermaths, funds for business trips, costs of building bases—it’s all money going out. However, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed had no proper way to make money. All they did was kill and plunder, but how much income could that have been? It was just like a drop in the ocean.

“Every day, it was just losses, losses, and losses!

“A massive creed like the Nine-Netherworlds Creed needed money for food, clothing, shelter, and travel. But spirit stones don’t grow on trees. Where were they supposed to find spirit stones?

“Those people below have no idea what was going on. They were delusional, talking about building an above-ground Nine-Netherworlds City. Forget whether the imperial court would find out—does the Nine-Netherworlds Creed even have the spirit stones to build a city?

“Can you imagine? Qin Haoran sat in the creed leader’s seat every day and handled all sorts of matters, and then he had to think of ways to make money.

“Whenever I dream, I view things from Qin Haoran’s eyes, sitting blankly with him and racking my brain to figure out how to make money.

“If not, I’d be facing the deficit data and numbers with Qin Haoran, attempting to find a way out. Now, just seeing numbers gives me a headache!

“Fortunately, Qin Haoran later met Yiren, who provided him a safe haven. Otherwise, I can’t even imagine how much more hellish Qin Haoran’s plight would have been.”

Li Haoran rubbed his temples in pain as he complained to the two.

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Why is this different from what we’d imagined?

Lu Yang recalled how Qin Haoran had met Su Yiren. Someone was hunting Qin Haoran down, causing him to be gravely injured. He crashed through a barrier and fainted in front of Su Yiren, and that sparked their subsequent fate with each other.

Previously, Lu Yang had deduced that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed was in turmoil, with a power grab happening and people ganging up to overthrow Qin Haoran.

But from what he had just heard, that no longer seemed to be the case.

“Then the people chasing Qin Haoran were...”

Li Haoran answered expressionlessly, “Debt collectors.”

Chapter 294: The Reason for Qin Haoran Being Hunted Down

“Debt collector” was a term Lu Yang was all too familiar with; he had a friend who fit that description.

“Why are you looking at me? I didn’t borrow any money!” Meng Jingzhou snapped angrily upon noticing Lu Yang’s gaze.

“Do you know which faction the debt collectors belonged to? Was it the Meng Family, the Luodi Merchant Guild, or some other group?” In Lu Yang's memory, the most prominent loan providers were these two factions: the wealthy Meng Family and the ubiquitous Luodi Merchant Guild.

Li Haoran shook his head. “I don’t know which faction it was. The dream fragments are always disjointed. A few days ago, I dreamed about the moment before Qin Haoran was severely injured. From their conversation, I learned that the other party was a debt collector and Qin Haoran had no money.

“But it’s not necessarily Qin Haoran who borrowed money. It could be that the entire Nine-Netherworlds Creed borrowed money, and the debt collectors went after the one in charge, in other words, the creed leader.”

Lu Yang was floored. “The other party knew that Qin Haoran was the leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?” They were so bold as to lend money to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?

If the Great Xia Dynasty finds out, they’ll be lucky to get away with just a layer of skin peeled off.

Li Haoran shook his head, stroking his chin as he analyzed. Through the repeated torment from Qin Haoran’s memories, his knowledge base was rapidly expanding. “They probably didn’t know. Based on the memory fragments I’ve obtained and my understanding of Qin Haoran, the most likely possibility is that Qin Haoran first withdrew a portion of spirit stones from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s treasury to register a small merchant guild, with its members being Qin Haoran and a few dozen people from the creed.

“After that, using some methods, probably short-term money-making schemes with long-term risks, he made it look like the small merchant guild’s business was booming. The few times the merchant guild borrowed money from the moneylenders, they would always repay on time. That way, when the moneylenders assessed this small merchant guild, they would perceive them as highly creditworthy, with a solid business and a future brimming with potential.

“The small merchant guild would then propose borrowing a huge sum to expand its operations, and the moneylenders were likely to agree. After obtaining the money, the merchant guild could spend all the spirit stones under the guise of business operations. In reality, they were secretly transferring all the spirit stones to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

“In the end, the small merchant guild declared bankruptcy.

“Since Qin Haoran registered the small merchant guild as a limited liability entity, its liability was limited to its contributed capital, and its members bear no personal liability. Thus, the creditors couldn’t directly claim their debts from Qin Haoran or other higher-ups of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.”

Li Haoran concluded, “In summary, Qin Haoran and the Nine-Netherworlds Creed borrowed money without having to repay it. It was a perfect plan.”

After hearing the story, Lu Yang felt that it seemed quite reasonable for the debt collectors to be hunting Qin Haoran down.

Understandable.

“Fortunately, Qin Haoran is dead, and his debts don’t fall on you,” Meng Jingzhou remarked, feeling relieved for Li Haoran. Otherwise, even if we sell Li Haoran, we won’t be able to repay the interest, let alone the debt.

“I hope so.” Li Haoran didn’t feel particularly comforted. This was one of the reasons he couldn’t sleep or eat in peace.

From a legal standpoint, I won’t inherit the debts of my past life, but whether the debt collectors will respect the law is another matter.

That troublemaker and deadweight Qin Haoran had it coming; good riddance!

Lu Yang patted Li Haoran’s shoulder. “Staying cooped up in your cave abode isn’t good. Why not go out for a change? Have you thought about how to form your golden core?”

Li Haoran shook his head. “No.”

In truth, he had Qin Haoran’s golden core formation method in his memories, but he didn’t want to follow Qin Haoran’s path.

“Perfect timing then. You should also form your golden core soon. Go out for a stroll for a change of mood. Who knows if you might find your fortuitous opportunity to form a golden core?

“With us two Golden Core experts protecting you, I guarantee nothing will go wrong on this trip!” Meng Jingzhou gave himself a thumbs-up, not forgetting that their original purpose in coming here was to show off their golden cores.

Li Haoran, “...”

So what if you’ve formed your golden cores? Think that makes you special? I have the cultivation epiphanies of an Apex Fusion expert; I’ll surpass you two sooner or later!

Yun Zhi had explicitly forbidden Li Haoran from leaving the Dao-Seeking Sect; otherwise, he would have gone to the jungle in search of opportunities to form his golden core.

There was only one circumstance in which Li Haoran could leave the Dao-Seeking Sect—if Lu Yang led him.

Lu Yang was a much safer option than Fifth Elder; they wouldn’t be scared even if they encountered an immortal.

“Let me inform my shifu before we leave.“

”Let's go.”

~~~

The three found Fifth Elder, who was forging artifacts. He held a massive hammer and hit the weapons, sending sparks flying everywhere. Every strike felt like mountains colliding, the earth shaking, and the ground trembling.

“Oh, it’s Haoran. What’s the matter?” Fifth Elder paused when he saw Li Haoran and the others approaching. He shrank the hammerhead and used it to massage his stiff back.

“Shifu, here’s the thing, I want to go out with Senior Brother Lu and Senior Brother Meng...” Li Haoran briefly explained his situation.

Fifth Elder nodded repeatedly, understanding Li Haoran’s predicament. It’s tantamount to Haoran having to deal with the various affairs of a major sect every day, and that is honestly distressing.

Otherwise, we wouldn’t have made the Taciturn Daoist Priest the sect leader.

“Junior Niece Yun Zhi said that if you go out with Lu Yang, nothing will go wrong. You may go.”

“Should we inform Big Senior Sister?” Li Haoran asked. He couldn’t help but feel guilty about leaving the sect.

“Big Senior Sister has something to attend to outside and won’t be back for a while,” Lu Yang said. I might be the only one in the entire Dao-Seeking Sect who knows what she’s up to.

The Xia Emperor had granted permission to relocate the immortal’s cave abode, and Yun Zhi had gone to move the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s kitchen. Moving it without damaging the integrity of the Everlasting Ruins was an exceedingly challenging task and required Yun Zhi to see to it herself.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was elated, giggling the whole day and unable to keep her mouth closed. She said that once the kitchen was moved back, she would definitely have to show off her skills to Lu Yang.

Lu Yang was too frightened to say anything.

~~~

After reporting to Fifth Elder, the three were about to board the vessel leaving the Dao-Seeking Sect when Lu Yang suddenly asked, “By the way, where are we headed?”

How can we buy tickets without knowing the destination?

The three exchanged blank glances at one another. They had been so focused on leaving the Dao-Seeking Sect that they hadn’t decided where to go.

We can’t just go back to the jungle, right?

“How about this? Let’s go to the Great Mission Hall and pick a mission. We’ll go wherever the mission takes us,” Li Haoran proposed. He happened to be short on contribution points.

“That works.” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou nodded, treating it as accompanying Li Haoran to earn contribution points.

Among the three, only Li Haoran lacked contribution points. Lu Yang had plenty of contribution points, and he could also use the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s contribution points at any time, while Meng Jingzhou could exchange spirit stones for contribution points.

~~~

Upon arriving at the Great Mission Hall, Meng Jingzhou immediately spotted a task he liked.

“Southern Ji Province, Shoutian[1] Commandery, Guhuai[2] Town. Outside the town is an abandoned temple where travelers often stop by. There are rumors of female ghosts that feed on yang energy haunting the area. Ever since word got out, travelers have been flocking there...”

“This is the one!” Meng Jingzhou slapped his thigh in excitement, feeling that he was fated for this mission.

It’s the perfect opportunity to test whether my Double Single’s Golden Core works!

Li Haoran rubbed his chin. Guhuai Town... why does this place sound so familiar?

1. It means something like “guard the fields.” ☜

2. It translates to “ancient locust tree.” ☜

Chapter 295: How Rumors Are Born

The imperial city was home to many oddly shaped buildings and structures. Some were the whimsical creations of formidable cultivators, others lacked artistic flair, and some served as symbols.

A bronze cauldron stood in a corner of the imperial city, towering like a small mountain. Its surface was as smooth as a mirror and adorned with intricate details. Even from a distance, one could sense its archaic beauty.

This was the most prosperous area of the imperial city, where every inch of land was worth its weight in gold. To place such a bronze cauldron here would cost an astronomical amount of spirit stones. Apart from a few major factions like the Luodi Merchant Guild, no one could afford such an expense.

Many elderly men with white hair and robes, emitting the fragrance of pills, strode into the bronze cauldron with their hands behind their backs. Nothing could seem to enter the eyes of these aloof men.

When passers-by saw them, their eyes would glimmer with reverence and envy. These elderly men were renowned masters in Pill Dao, many of whom had pioneered their own methods of pill concoction.

This was the Pill Concoction Alliance, representing the prestige and pinnacle of the Pill Dao. Every year, countless pill formulas were released to the public, showcasing their remarkable achievements. It was a sacred place for all pill-concocting masters, second only to the Pill Cauldron Peak of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

~~~

Inside the bronze cauldron, reticent pill-concocting masters set around an exquisite stone table, their faces completely devoid of emotions.

A figure arrived late, signaling the commencement of the meeting. freeweɓnøvel.com

He was the Clear Clouds[1] Doyen,[2] the chief pill-concocting master of the Pill Concoction Alliance. With his superlative skills, he was fully deserving of being the top pill-concocting master.

Everyone seated here was a veteran in the pill-concocting community, each possessing unique abilities, but all acknowledged the Clear Clouds Doyen’s status. Even the proud Seventh Elder admitted that the Clear Clouds Doyen was second only to him in pill concoction.

The Clear Clouds Doyen smiled faintly and addressed the audience at a measured pace. “As usual, this meeting is for the exchange of pill-concocting insights. Please feel free to speak your mind.”

“Can we really say anything?” A pill-concocting master raised his hand and asked.

“Yes.”

The pill-concocting master’s expression instantly changed, and he slammed the table in rage. “Clear Clouds Doyen, you’re late! Who are you putting on an act for? We’ve been sitting here waiting for you all day!”

Clearly, acknowledging the Clear Clouds Doyen's status in the pill concoction world didn’t signify that they could tolerate his tardiness.

“Apologies, apologies. I was studying a pill formula and made a major breakthrough. I got so excited that I lost track of time.

“What pill were you studying that got you so engrossed?”

The Clear Clouds Doyen smiled mysteriously. “An ancient pill formula—the Child-Gifting Pill.”

“You successfully concocted it?!” The crowd was astonished. They had the formula for the Child-Gifting Pill, but no matter how they tried to concoct it, the resultant product could only enhance their Dao partners’ beauty and complexion.

Recently, many beauty-enhancing pills had been circulating on the black market—these were the failed pills they had produced, which had no use other than improving the appearance of those who ingested them.

“Not yet, but I already have a general idea. According to my research, the owner of the Child-Gifting Pill is Qing He, and she seems to have a close connection with a certain immortal. Perhaps the Child-Gifting Pill is also related to this immortal!”

“To think it’s related to an immortal! That does make sense.” Despite the crowd’s initial surprise, they soon internalized it—one of the ingredients was an immortal fruit, which explained why they couldn’t replicate it.

“Hmph, and here I thought it was some major breakthrough. Is that all?” Seventh Elder snorted disdainfully at the Clear Cloud Doyen’s so-called research.

“I was wondering who it is. So, it’s Wuji Doyen[3] of Pill Cauldron Peak. What brilliant insights do you have?” When the Clear Clouds Doyen saw that it was Seventh Elder, his unruffled countenance vanished, his tone laced with belligerent sarcasm.

The Clear Clouds Doyen and Seventh Elder locked eyes, the tension in the air palpable. The others didn’t know what to say; everyone knew the history between the two.

In their younger days, both had fallen for the same girl. After a fight, which mainly involved Seventh Elder pinning the Clear Clouds Doyen to the ground and beating him, the girl ultimately chose the talented Seventh Elder.

And thus, their feud began.

Since Seventh Elder often concocted strange pills, it was hard for others to judge his true pill-concocting skills. But one thing was certain—when it came to combat, none of those present were a match for Seventh Elder.

Seventh Elder slowly said, “According to my research, the key to the pill formula isn’t the pill itself but the consumption method. Have you noticed? The pill formula begins with the instructions for consumption: ‘When taken with river water, it can induce pregnancy.’

“Why specifically mention ‘river water?’ Why not just state ‘water?’

“With this question in mind, I scoured ancient texts and consulted young scholars knowledgeable about the ancient era. Finally, I found the answer.

“The ‘river water’ mentioned in this pill formula isn’t ordinary river water but the water of the Mother-Child River, created by an immortal during ancient times!

“Drinking the water of the Mother-Child River can induce pregnancy!”

The atmosphere crackled with shock.

“What?!”

“Mother-Child Water?”

“There’s such a mystical river?!”

Although Seventh Elder often refines strange pills, he never joked about something like this!

“Which immortal was it?” the Clear Clouds Doyen asked eagerly, forgetting his enmity with Seventh Elder.

He had searched through ancient texts and even borrowed rare books from the imperial palace, but he couldn’t find the name of that immortal. It was as if it had been deliberately concealed!

Seventh Elder nodded solemnly. “It was the Heaven Mandate Immortal.”

The Clear Clouds Doyen suddenly understood. “So it was him? That explains everything.”

“How so?” Everyone was baffled. We haven’t heard anything about the Heaven-Mandate Immortal refining the Mother-Child River though?

The Clear Clouds Doyen spoke with an air of mystery. “I found an ancient text called the Comprehensive Culinary Compendium in a ruin. Although I have yet to fully decipher it, I can be certain of one thing—this book may appear to teach cooking, but there is more than meets the eye.”

The crowd was bewildered. The title sounds like an ancient cookbook. Is it not?

“At first, I was like all of you and thought it was an ancient cookbook. But when I casually prepared a few dishes, I discovered that anyone who ate them would at least fall into a coma.

“This is not a cookbook—it’s a poison codex!”

Everyone gasped. An ancient poison codex? That sounds terrifying.

“And the author of this poison codex was none other than the Heaven Mandate Immortal!

“Pills and poison are two sides of the same coin. If the Heaven Mandate Immortal could write this poison codex, he must have also been well-versed in pill concoction!

“I have heard of an ancient saying: the greatest pill-concocting master doesn’t search for medicinal ingredients but invents them! The Mother-Child River must have been a medicinal ingredient the Heaven Mandate Immortal created!

“Wait, no, perhaps the Mother-River Child’s water was not a medicinal ingredient but poison!“

The Clear Clouds Doyen’s eyes lit up. “If you use water from the Mother-Child River as poison during battles, wouldn’t the opponent become pregnant and rendered unable to fight?” He felt that his analysis was logical and seamlessly interlinked, as if he had unraveled yet another veil of mystery from the ancient era.

“How many women must have become pregnant due to the Heaven Mandate Immortal refining the water of the Mother-Child River?” The crowd marveled at the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s power.

As expected of an immortal to be capable of crafting something as mystical as this.

After the servant boy poured water for everyone, he quietly left. With the room filled with pill-concocting masters and their discussions revolving around immortals, he was too frightened to stay.

As soon as he stepped outside, he was surrounded by his companions.

“So, how did it go? What did they say inside?”

This was the most elite summit of pill-concocting masters, representing the forefront of knowledge in the pill-concocting world. Hearing even a modicum of their meeting would be enough for them to boast about.

The servant boy was in a tough spot; he had been too scared earlier and hadn’t listened carefully. He tried hard to recall the conversation of the pill-concocting masters and hesitantly replied, “I think they said that the ancient immortal, the Heaven Mandate Immortal, made countless women pregnant?”

His companions inhaled sharply.

This is truly an ancient secret.

1. Although it can refer to the clouds high up in the sky, it is often used as a metaphor for high rank and status as well as lofty morals. ☜

2. His name is Qingyun-zi in Chinese. There will be a short note on “子” or “zi” in Chinese below. ☜

3. Wuji is a concept in Chinese philosophy that is often said to be the origin of Taiji and Qigong. ☜

Chapter 296: Three Scholars

In Guhuai Town, located in Shoutian Commandery, stood an abandoned temple.

In the southern part of Ji Province, a torrential downpour had turned the green grass into a quagmire. The emerald leaves stood vertically in the rain, their vitality washed away by the rain.

The sky was a blanket of dull gray, oppressive and suffocating, as if darkness could descend at any moment.

A scholar clad in a straw raincoat and hat hurried along, clutching a bundle of books wrapped in cloth as he madly dashed through the tempest of rain.

Spotting an abandoned temple not far away, his eyes sparkled. He tightened his grip on the books and quickened his pace, sprinting toward the temple.

Huffing and puffing, the scholar closed the doors and windows. Though the temple was dilapidated, it was fortunate that it wasn’t leaking.

He unwrapped the bundle to check if the books had gotten wet. Perhaps because he had protected them well, the books were still dry.

The scholar lit an oil lamp and began to read softly by its dim light.

Suddenly, a graceful figure appeared behind the scholar. With an alluring smile, she tapped him on the back.

Upon seeing the figure, the scholar seemed entranced, involuntarily smiling.

After the heavy rain stopped, the weary scholar left the abandoned temple.

~~~

Three figures dressed as scholars trudged through the morass, their steps uneven and their appearance quite disheveled.

“Why is this road so difficult to walk on?” one of the figures complained.

Another figure rolled his eyes. “Just deal with it. Learn to be content. Isn’t this much better than when we were in the jungle?”

“True.”

The third figure explained, “I heard that a once-in-a-decade downpour drenched Guhuai Town yesterday, causing the river to overflow its banks. It’s said that it’ll rain again tonight.”

“Tsk, that doesn’t seem like a good omen.”

Lu Yang pointed at the temple and smiled. “Perfect then. There’s a temple ahead. Although it’s a bit run-down, the Buddha statue should still be inside. You can go and pay your respects when we stay the night.

“Let’s go over the plan again. Based on the available intelligence, the target is highly cautious and won’t easily reveal herself. Moreover, she’s a ghost soul with excellent escape techniques, making her hard to capture.

“The female ghost’s strength should be at the Foundation Establishment Stage, though her exact cultivation realm is unclear. If she shows herself, we must make sure she can’t escape before moving in to catch her!

“Our current identities are scholars heading to the imperial city to seek honor and prestige. We will stay here for the night and use this opportunity to lure the female ghost out!

“So far, there’s been no news of the female ghost killing anyone. When we capture her, don’t go for the kill.

“In the past, I had no experience traveling outside. But after seeing my shifu imprisoned, I learned the importance of using fake names in the outside world. That way, even if we embarrass ourselves, we won’t bring shame to the real us in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Let’s confirm our names once more. I am Lu Yiyang.”

“I am Long Jingzhou.”

“I am Li Hao.”

After a discussion, the three felt that the plan was sound. They concealed their auras as much as possible and disguised themselves as mortals before entering the temple.

“This temple is so clean.” Meng Jingzhou was surprised. He had expected the place to be covered in dust, with spiderwebs in every corner.

The interior of the temple was far beyond his expectations. It was as speckless as if someone had recently cleaned it.

The only regret was that the Buddha statue in the center was missing its upper half, so they couldn't pay their respects.

Li Haoran found some dry firewood behind the Buddha statue, likely left by the last person who stayed here. He piled the firewood together and gathered some dry grass. Pulling out a flint from his bag, he lit a fire.

As he warmed his hands by the fire, an expression of pure comfort spread across his face. “Whew—I feel alive again.”

Lu Yang took out a few mantou[1] buns from his bag, skewered them with wooden sticks, and roasted them over the fire.

When the mantou’s outer skin turned slightly golden, he broke one of the mantou apart. The aroma mixed with the steam wafted toward them.

Meng Jingzhou walked around the temple and returned to the main hall. “Aside from the main hall, there are two other rooms. We can each take one when it’s time to sleep later.”

“Alright.”

The three sat around the fire, eating the mantou with jiangcai pickles[2] while lamenting the difficult road ahead.

Lu Yang was plagued with worry, and even the mantou in his hand didn’t taste fragrant anymore. “I wonder if our journey to the imperial capital will go smoothly. I’ve heard that cultivators are everywhere in the imperial capital. For us mortals, making a name for ourselves there will only be even more difficult.”

Meng Jingzhou waved his hand. “The number of cultivators in the imperial capital isn’t as exaggerated as you think. At most, one in twenty people is a cultivator. Becoming a cultivator is incredibly tough. The test of spirit root alone already eliminates ninety-nine percent of people.”

One cultivator in twenty people was already an astonishing ratio. No other major city in the Central Continent could rival this.

“Although we don’t have spirit roots, we have our knowledge. We can effortlessly write essays and possess unique insights into current affairs and politics. Tomorrow, we will leave Shoutian Commandery, head to the capital for the imperial examinations, seek honor and prestige, gain the emperor’s favor, and secure an official position. It’s not completely impossible.”

Not all ranked officials in the Great Xia Dynasty were cultivators; some were mortals.

Meng Jingzhou pointed at Li Haoran with his mantou. “For instance, Brother Li, you memorized the Thousand Character Classic[3] at age five, wrote free-style shi poetry at age seven, composed lyrical ci poetry[4] at age eight, and wrote essays at age ten. You’re brimming with talent, and your writing is splendid as if it were the work of nature. Even your teacher couldn’t stop complimenting you, praising you as the best student he has ever taught.”

Li Haoran smiled modestly. “Brother Long, you flatter me. My teacher simply wanted to encourage me, hence the appraisal. On the other hand, Brother Long, you’re giving up your family business to seek a future in the imperial city. Such confidence is something Brother Lu and I can’t match.”

The three lavished praises on one another, then flipped through the classics written by the saints and sages, reading with keen interest. They marveled at the impressive work of the past sages, who they believed were truly deserving of their timeless fame.

If we could write even one essay like that, we’d die without regrets.

Meng Jingzhou yawned, ruthlessly crushing Lu Yang’s dreams. “Alright, stop dreaming and go to sleep. We have to get up early tomorrow.”

As agreed while eating the mantou, the three entered their respective rooms. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou took the rooms on both sides, while Li Haoran stayed in the main hall, sleeping in front of the half-destroyed Buddha statue.

In the darkness, three graceful figures watched the trio, their eyes faintly glowing green.

“Three more people have arrived. Their yang energy is so abundant. Ah, I really want to know what they taste like...” The figure in cyan robes tittered.

“Exactly! It’s been so long since we’ve seen scholars with such vibrant yang energy. Although scholars who read classics by sages for a long time can develop vast righteous qi, it’s rare to see ones like these three.” The figure in red robes licked her seductive red lips.

The figure in white, who appeared younger, hurriedly said, “Elder Sisters, you must be careful not to drain all their yang energy. We need to adopt a sustainable approach to tackling problems.

“If they find it comfortable the first time, they’ll come back for a second time. Over time, we’ll absorb more yang energy than if we absorb it all at once.”

“Got it, got it. Little Seven, you’re the youngest but also the most long-winded. We know where to draw the line. If we go overboard, we’ll attract the attention of the righteous path, and we’ll be the ones in trouble; we get that.

“Let’s split up. The two of us will go to the rooms on either side. Little Seven, you stay here and attend to this Li guy.”

2. It’s a specific type of Chinese pickle consisting of vegetables and fruits in sauces such as soy sauce. There are many varieties, but here’s a simple image. ☜ freewēbnovel.com
