Chapter 297: LI Haoran Is Probably a Goner

In the side room, Lu Yang lit an oil lamp and concentrated on reading, completely oblivious to the cyan-robed, graceful figure that had appeared in the room.

Though Lu Yang appeared to be reading, he was actually communicating with an immortal in his mental space.

“Hmm? Lu Yang, you have committed so many evil deeds that you were expelled from the Dao-Seeking Sect and have been reduced to living in a place like this?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was overjoyed, gloating over his misfortune.

“...Immortal Fairy, your imagination doesn’t need to be this vivid. Besides, others measure their sleep in hours, but why do you measure yours in days?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy placed her hands on her hips and pouted. “How can immortals be the same as mortals?”

“Yes yes yes, Your Excellency Immortal Fairy is not like everyone else. So, can you go back to sleep now? I have things to do.”

“What things?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s interest was piqued.

Seeing that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wouldn’t rest until she heard the whole story, Lu Yang had no choice but to explain everything.

“So you are now luring the female ghost here to capture her?”

“Yes.”

“That’s simple. Leave it to me.” With a confident pat on her chest, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy seemed emboldened by the power of the Unbeatable Golden Core.

Since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was in the state of a soul—essentially a ghost soul—she was perfectly suited for the current situation.

“Wait, Immortal Fairy, aren’t you scared of ghosts?” Lu Yang remembered how petrified the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been when they visited the tomb built by First Elder, fearing that ghosts would spring out.

“Why would I be scared of ghosts I can see... wait, no, I’m not scared of ghosts at all!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy realized she had slipped up and quickly corrected herself.

“Alright, but don’t take things too far!” Lu Yang warned before handing over control of his body to her.

“Young Sir~~ I’m so lonely, won’t you keep me company~~” The cyan-robed figure appeared in front of Lu Yang, gazing at him with affection, her voice so sweet it could numb one’s bones.

Little did she know, the Lu Yang before her was now a different Lu Yang.

She saw “Lu Yang” flash a devilish smile and reach out to pull her into his embrace.

The cyan-robed figure was momentarily stunned. This doesn’t seem like the person I had seen in the main hall earlier.

“Lu Yang” extended his index finger to lift her chin and said flirtatiously, “Lonely little beauty, do you need elder sister to keep you company?”

“Lu Yang” hugged the cyan-robed figure intimately, his hands roaming up and down. “You look good, but your figure isn’t as good as mine.”

What do you mean my figure isn’t as good as yours? And why are you calling yourself “elder sister?”

This person doesn’t seem like she’s a woman disguised as a man either?

The cyan-robed figure could feel her hair prick up. I have met a pervert.

“Come, little beauty. The night is short, so come play with elder sister,” giggled “Lu Yang,” who looked nothing like a good person.

The cyan-robed figure wanted to escape, only to find the other party’s grip terrifyingly strong. Despite being a Foundation Establishment cultivator, she couldn’t struggle free.

“Hehe, trying to run?” Lu Yang pounced toward the cyan-robed figure.

Inside the mental space, the real Lu Yang pounced toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Huang Doudou, you jerk! What are you trying to do with my body?!”

“I'm just having some fun. I won’t do anything serious.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy took to her heels.

“That won’t do either! It’ll ruin my image!”

~~~

Meng Jingzhou pretended to be asleep and snoring, trying to suppress the smile at the corner of his mouth as he quietly waited for the female ghost to arrive.

The female ghost appeared beside Meng Jingzhou’s bed, dressed in red like a bride on her wedding day.

The red-robed female ghost blew a breath toward Meng Jingzhou, making him dazed.

“My Dear Lord, wake up,” the red-robed ghost gently whispered in Meng Jingzhou’s ear.

Meng Jingzhou woke up groggily, looking at the red-robed ghost with hesitation. “You are?”

“My Dear Lord, have you forgotten? I’m your wife.”

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes lit up. The Double Single’s Golden Core is working! This ghost is claiming to be my wife despite just meeting me!

Don’t be impatient, don’t be impatient. Stay calm.

Then, the dazed expression returned to his face.

The red-robed female ghost’s rosy lips inched closer to Meng Jingzhou, and his heart pounded with excitement.

Bang!

Before the red-robed ghost’s lips could touch Meng Jingzhou, an invisible energy on the surface of his body sent her flying. She fell unconscious, her lips swollen like sausages from the scorching energy, stripped of all their former beauty.

The Single’s Golden Core was like the sun, upright and unyielding. It resided in the middle of the dantian and commanded all directions. Evil beings such as demons and ghosts could not approach.

The effect of the Double Single’s Golden Core was naturally even stronger.

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

The female ghost couldn’t even touch me.

~~~

In the main hall, Li Haoran lay in front of the half-destroyed Buddha statue, monitoring his surroundings with his five senses. He dared not act rashly, lest the female ghost notice.

She’s here!

The white-robed figure quietly approached Li Haoran, unaware that her every move had already been detected by him.

Fwoosh— The white-robed figure exhaled a cold breath, sending chills down Li Haoran’s spine.

Li Haoran got a huge fright upon seeing the ghost. “Who are you?”

The white-robed ghost said softly, “Benefactor, there’s no need to panic. I’m just a powerless wandering ghost. I was hoping to borrow some of your yang energy.” She put on a pitiful, harmless appearance.

Li Haoran clearly didn’t buy her ghost of a story.[1] What “powerless?” Her ghost soul is solid, her consciousness is clear, and she is even emanating indistinct traces of power.

Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.

What ghostly hellish luck is this?[2] Even the ghost I run into is at the same level as me.

“I’ll make sure you feel comfortable, Benefactor,” the white-robed ghost purred in a bewitching voice, making one’s heart itch.

Li Haoran found it strange. By now, there should have been some commotion from Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou catching the ghost. Why hasn’t there been any noise?

Did something go wrong?

Li Haoran decided not to expose the female ghost’s lies and instead played along to extract some information.

“Why does a ghost need yang energy? To return to life in the yang realm?”[3]

“Benefactor, you jest. Ghosts cannot return to life. We only collect a bit of yang energy to survive.”

While flirting, the white-robed female ghost climbed onto Li Haoran, and the two locked eyes.

Suddenly, the door to the main hall was flung open, and a young girl barged in.

“I’m sorry, is anyone here? I’ve run out of travel funds. Could I stay here for the night?”

The girl was tall and dressed in plain clothes. Despite traveling outside, she carried no cloth-bundled baggage with her. Despite the mire around the temple, there wasn’t a speck of mud on her shoes.

Li Haoran and the white-robed female ghost both turned to look at the girl who had just arrived.

The girl was also startled by the scene before her. This was her first time traveling outside. Is the outside world this open? They even play in a decrepit temple?

She felt awkward, not expecting to encounter such a situation. No matter how inexperienced she was, she knew this was something she should avoid to give the involved parties some privacy.

Just as she instinctively turned her head to leave, she noticed that the man lying on the ground looked familiar.

She silently walked forward, confirming that she wasn’t mistaken.

Looking down at Li Haoran with a fake smile, she asked in a voice even gentler than the female ghost’s, “Ex-dad, what are you doing?”

Li Haoran swallowed a mouthful of saliva, feeling that he was probably a goner.

This young girl was none other than Qin Yanyan, Li Haoran’s daughter from his past life.

1. ”Nonsense” in Chinese is made up of the characters “ghost” and “speech,” so I have tried to incorporate the wordplay here. ☜

2. Similarly, the cursing here also contains the character for “ghost.” ☜

3. The phrase here actually contains the same character “yang.” ☜

Chapter 298: Ex-Dad

Ex-dad—referring to a dad from an ex-lifetime—was a novel and unique form of address for Li Haoran.[1]

Qin Yanyan had set out to travel the world, seeking fortuitous opportunities to form her golden core and comprehend the mortal world, striving for a breakthrough in her mental state.

She had only passed through a few commanderies and counties and decided to stay overnight in this dilapidated temple, yet she had already stumbled upon such an exhilarating situation.

After her mother persuaded her for a month, Qin Yanyan was just beginning to accept Li Haoran as her father despite sharing no blood relations with him.

I don’t think this is exactly how one is supposed to comprehend the mortal world.

“Wait, Yanyan, let me explain!” Li Haoran panicked. Heaven and earth, I swear on my conscience that I’m truly here to catch ghosts. Before I could extract any useful information, Qin Yanyan caught me red-handed.

The Central Continent is so vast. How did Qin Yanyan still run into me?

Is this the karmic entanglement between father and daughter?

The white-robed female ghost sensed something was amiss and tried to escape.

Li Haoran used Grappling Hand, transitioning between the tangible and intangible states as he pinned the ghost to the ground. This was a skill he had just learned while refining artifacts. With a slight alteration, he had adapted it to catching ghosts.

Despite also being at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, the female ghost was no match for Li Haoran.

Li Haoran quickly explained, “I received a mission from the sect to catch ghosts with Senior Brother Lu and Senior Brother Meng!” If I let Qin Yanyan walk away with this misunderstanding and pass it to Su Yiren, I won’t have to inherit Qin Haoran’s memories anymore—I can just start my tenth life right away.

“Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou?” Qin Yanyan recalled the two prodigies from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

One is the disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect Leader, and the other is the eldest young master of the Meng Family. They’re naturally much more credible than Li Haoran.

“That’s right! They’re sleeping in the rooms next door. They can definitely prove my innocence!” As Li Haoran defended himself, he used a refined Soul-Locking Chain to bind the white-robed ghost to a wooden pillar before going to find Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Qin Yanyan was skeptical as she followed Li Haoran to look for the other two.

Li Haoran pushed the door open, speaking at a frightening speed. “Brother Lu, you must prove my innocence. We’re here to catch ghosts, right? You haven’t given the signal to act because the female ghost didn’t come to you...”

Before he could finish, he saw the corners of Lu Yang’s mouth carry an odd smile as he tugged at the cyan-robed female ghost. The latter struggled desperately but to no avail, her face filled with despair; she could only let Lu Yang do as he wished with her.

This scene looks nothing like what a righteous gentleman would do.

“Senior Brother Lu, you...” Li Haoran stuttered. I never expected Lu Yang to be someone like this.

Upon witnessing this scene, Qin Yanyan felt that Li Haoran was making excuses and flew into a rage. “And you still dared to say you’re here to catch ghosts?!”

“Let’s go check on Senior Brother Meng. He must be working hard to catch ghosts!” Li Haoran was certain there would be no surprises with Meng Jingzhou. With his Single’s Spirit Root, even if his brain can think of ideas, his body can’t act on them.

Then, Qin Yanyan saw the unconscious red-robed female ghost with Meng Jingzhou squatting beside her and observing her intently.

“Date rape?!”

Color drained from Qin Yanyan’s face. Why is it getting more and more outrageous?

Comparing the three, Li Haoran seems to be the most conservative.

Li Haoran, “...”

Why does nothing good ever happen when I go out with Senior Brother Lu and Senior Brother Meng? Last time, I ended up with a fiancée three thousand years older than me and a daughter with no blood relation, while I became the former leader of one of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds.

This time, when I need you to prove my innocence, the two of you just have to pull this kind of stunt on me.

“Rubbish! Date rape? Don’t you know I have a Single’s Spirit Root?!” Meng Jingzhou snapped in anger and turned around. Let me see who has such poor judgment.

“Eh, elder niece, you’re here to look for your dad?”

Qin Yanyan sensed the aura of a Golden Core cultivator emanating from Meng Jingzhou and repeatedly warned herself that she couldn’t defeat him.

Meanwhile, Lu Yang finally subdued the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and regained control of his body, dragging the cyan-robed female ghost over to find Li Haoran and Meng Jingzhou.

After the three presented the mission issued by the sect and Meng Jingzhou revealed his Single’s Spirit Root, Qin Yanyan finally believed the trio were here to catch ghosts instead of visiting prostitutes.

The cyan-robed ghost trembled like a leaf. These three are from the Dao-Seeking Sect, one of the Five Great Immortal Sects?!

Everyone headed back to the main hall. Li Haoran tied the still-trembling cyan-robed ghost and the unconscious red-robed ghost next to the white-robed ghost.

With that, all three female ghosts were captured.

“So, you’re saying that the Dao-Seeking Sect posted a ghost-catching mission, and you came to Guhuai Town to catch ghosts to complete the mission?” By now, Qin Yanyan had largely accepted their account of the story.

She still didn’t know that her former father was the reincarnation of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s leader. Li Haoran had only gained fragments of Qin Haoran’s memories after Su Yiren and Qin Yanyan had left.

This is not something I can explain to Qin Yanyan easily.

I mean, I can’t possibly just say, “Your father in his past life was the leader of a diabolic creed and was a bad egg.” That would really cause our father-daughter relationship to collapse.

“What about you? Why did you come to Guhuai Town?”

“Mother said that the last time I went to your house, I immediately started arguing and was too impatient, so I need to improve my mental state. As it happened, it was also time for me to form my golden core, so she suggested that I go out for a walk to train my mental state.

“Earlier today, I was in Shoutian Commandery. I wandered around the merchant guild and spent all my travel funds. Since there were no free inns in Shoutian Commandery, I could only keep heading north. When I saw this ancient temple here, I thought I’d stay here for the night. And here I am now.”

Li Haoran was deeply concerned about Qin Yanyan’s travel journey and experience.

In a few days, I’m afraid Qin Yanyan might find herself performing on the streets for a living.

“F-four great heroes, although we are ghosts, we have never harmed anyone!” the green-robed ghost cried out in grievance.

They had conscientiously absorbed yang energy without stirring up trouble, fearing it would attract righteous cultivators. Unfortunately, what you fear always comes true. And this time, it’s the Dao-Seeking Sect, the strongest of the righteous sects. I heard that righteous cultivators loathe demons and ghosts, killing every single one on sight.

Now that we have fallen into their hands, can we even survive?

“You have never harmed anyone?” Meng Jingzhou sneered. “The mission clearly stated that you absorbed people’s yang energy until they became listless and dazed all day. Don’t tell me all of that is false?”

The white-robed female ghost was on the verge of tears. “It’s really not true. We absorb the yang energy very carefully, only taking a small amount that doesn’t affect people. Moreover, the matter of our yang energy absorption has been registered with the town mayor.

“We also know that absorbing too much would have adverse effects on people. If we did that, who could come back? It’s better to absorb a little over multiple times than to suck someone dry all at once. We understand the principle of not draining the pond to get at the fish and killing the goose that lays the golden eggs.”

“Hold on, the town mayor knows about this?”

“Not just the town mayor; even the travelers in town can testify!” the white-robed ghost declared with conviction.

Lu Yang and the others were completely flummoxed.

“It’s true, we’re not lying to you. Earlier, the three of us sisters went around knocking on the doors of various inns and asking if anyone needed our services. After finishing one round of service, we returned and saw you three heroes lying in the temple. Seeing that your yang energy was quite strong, we thought we’d absorb a bit as the finale for tonight.”

Question marks were popping out of Lu Yang’s head.

You even offer door-to-door service?!

The white-robed ghost said sheepishly, “Good service brings repeat customers.”

Qin Yanyan was even more flabbergasted than Lu Yang. Is this what the mundane world is like?

1. “Former dad” may be more correct, referring to one’s father from their past life. However, due to how it sounds like ex-girlfriend and ex-boyfriend and the like in Chinese, I decided to opt for “ex-dad.” ☜

Chapter 299: The Hardworking Female Ghosts

“You said the town mayor knows about this. Do you dare to come with us to see him?” Li Haoran didn’t believe their ghostly nonsense, hoping to see a trace of fear in their expressions.

Unfortunately, he saw none.

The four humans and three ghosts waited the entire night in the dilapidated temple. As the sky began to turn bright, with the moon emitting a soft glow and gradually transitioning into the sun, they set off to visit the town mayor.

Guhuai Town was famous for its locust trees. They could be seen everywhere, and most were up in years. The thickest old locust tree was so massive that even three Lu Yangs couldn’t wrap their arms around it.

The white-robed ghost, who called herself Little Seven, told them that this ancient locust tree was over a thousand years old, older than the town itself.

Locust trees were of a yin nature, so the entire town had a gloomy atmosphere with cool weather, making it an excellent summer retreat.

Among the towns Lu Yang had been to, Guhuai Town could be considered the largest. Moreover, Guhuai Town appeared to be flourishing, with a momentum that seemed likely to carry into the future.

~~~

After the four announced their identities at the yamen, the town mayor quickly came out to greet them. He was somewhat portly and wore a cheerful smile for everyone. “I didn’t expect Daoists from the Dao-Seeking Sect to come here. My apologies for not welcoming you properly.” The town mayor displayed a humble attitude.

Lu Yang noticed that the town mayor was at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.

When the town mayor spotted the three female ghosts behind the four, his expression changed slightly, but he soon composed himself and introduced himself politely, “My surname is Fan, and my full name is Fan Guiren.[1] You can call me Little Fan.

“Please, come in.”

“You’re too polite, Town Mayor Fan.” Lu Yang took a sip of the tea Town Mayor Fan had poured and nodded slightly.

Mmm, I can’t tell what kind of tea this is.

“Town Mayor Fan, you probably know why we’re here. We wish to understand the full story of these three female ghosts.”

“As I thought.” Town Mayor Fan’s head drooped dejectedly. To be honest, I don’t really want to discuss this matter, but since the people from the Dao-Seeking Sect have asked me, it’s not like I can refuse them.

Lu Yang went straight to the point. “Are you aware that these three female ghosts are absorbing human yang energy, Town Mayor Fan?”

“Yes, I am. Back then, a traveler came to report a case of female ghosts absorbing human yang energy in the abandoned temple outside the town. After hearing about it, I thought it was a serious matter and immediately led people there to investigate.

“Only when we arrived at the temple did I learn that Little Seven and the other two ghosts weren’t the kind of wicked ghosts that drain people’s yang energy all at once. Instead, they are good ghosts with no intention of harming humans.

“At that time, Guhuai Town wasn’t as bustling as it is today. I wanted to develop the tourism industry to increase the town’s income, but a bunch of locust trees alone couldn’t attract visitors.

“That was when I thought of the female ghosts. Worried about potential complications, I even checked the laws and found that while it was prohibited for female ghosts to cause harm to humans or disrupt their lives through absorbing yang energy, absorbing yang energy itself wasn’t completely banned.

“Since female ghosts absorbing yang energy isn’t considered prostitution, that means that travelers don’t even have to pay. Furthermore, the tax regulations don’t mention that ghosts absorbing yang energy are required to pay taxes.

“After repeated deliberation, I decided to use the female ghosts as a gimmick to promote Guhuai Town. And you know what? It worked pretty well. Many travelers came to seek romantic encounters with beautiful women, and the town’s income visibly surged. Local finances were on an upswing, the commandery rewarded us, and I became well-off, allowing me to advance to the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage smoothly.

“Originally, the commandery had intentions to promote me, but being the town mayor here, I get plenty of food, drinks, and spirit stones, which is better than being a subordinate in the commandery, so I declined. Even if I get promoted to the commandery, it’ll have to wait until I reach the Golden Core Stage.” Town Mayor Fan had a clear plan for his political career.

The three female ghosts nodded repeatedly, expressing that they were innocent and good ghosts.

“Wait, if this is a good thing, who reported it to our sect and said there were female ghosts here?” Meng Jingzhou was puzzled.

The Dao-Seeking Sect didn’t uncover this mission themselves; someone had reported it to them.

A competitor?

This industry has competitors?

Town Mayor Fan was also surprised. He had thought that Lu Yang and the other two had just happened to pass by, discovered the female ghosts, and decided to subdue them.

How could it have been reported?

“Town Mayor Fan, do you have any leads?”

“Not yet... By the way, could I ask what the mission description reads?”

“It mentioned that there are female ghosts absorbing human yang energy in Guhuai Town, causing scholars to become lethargic and listless.”

Town Mayor Fan’s expression became peculiar.

“Town Mayor Fan, do you know what’s going on?”

Town Mayor Fan nodded. “Scholar Zhou[2] has a son, whom everyone calls Little Zhou. Little Zhou’s academic performance is average, and he’s failed the xiucai[3] scholar exam several times.

“But Little Zhou’s mother always thought it was because her son kept visiting the female ghosts, which distracted him and made him too lethargic to study properly. Little Zhou’s mother came looking for me, hoping I would punish the female ghosts, but everyone knew Little Zhou’s academic level. He’s naturally playful and can’t focus on studying. It had nothing to do with the female ghosts.

“I simply thought she was being unreasonable and ignored her. After Little Zhou’s mother left, a few others blamed the female ghosts for their children’s failure to pass the imperial exams, but I refuted them all.

“I didn’t expect they’d be so persistent and report this to the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Town Mayor Fan sighed. “Little Seven and the others have already tried their best.”

Little Seven chimed in. “We three sisters were afraid this matter would blow up and attract the attention of the righteous sects, so we invited the underperforming scholars in town to the temple to offer them lessons. Since the three of us were from scholarly families when we were alive, teaching them was not a problem at all.

“If they studied well, they’d get rewards. If they didn’t, they’d get nothing. Under this reward and punishment scheme, their grades improved tremendously.”

Lu Yang sized up the three female ghosts. The red-robed ghost’s lips are as swollen as sausages, so I’ll leave her aside for now.

The white-robed and cyan-robed ghosts are both attractive and dressed lightly, each with their distinct charm. How could those scholars focus on studying?

Oh right, if they didn’t study, they wouldn’t get rewards.

“The scholars were also willing to study in this manner. Take yesterday, for example. The once-in-a-decade downpour turned the day as dark as night. Yet, Little Zhou and the others still braved the rain to attend our lectures. They kept studying until the rain stopped, finally leaving the temple mentally and physically exhausted.

“Who would have thought that despite all our efforts, their parents still reported us?” Life is too tough. It doesn’t matter whether you’re alive or dead.

Lu Yang summarized, “So, during the day, you run a private school and teach students, and at night, you wander the town and absorb yang energy at inns?”

“That’s right.”

Lu Yang and the other two felt ashamed. The female ghosts are even more diligent than us.

Qin Yanyan listened in amazement. So this is what ghosts are like?

Little Seven continued, “Not just that. We have to hand over seventy percent of the yang energy we absorb. Only thirty percent is ours to keep.”

“Hmm? Who do you hand it over to?” Lu Yang was bewildered. The imperial court doesn’t need yang energy.

“It’s our superior. We call him Lord Mi. Lord Mi also mentioned that there’s some treasure left behind by some previous creed leader in Guhuai Town and told us to keep an eye out for it.”

1. The “guiren” here literally means a noble or a person of high rank. For a moment, I did a double take and wondered whether it was his name or title. ☜

2. Although it is translated as “scholar” in English, there are in fact many levels to scholars, and their titles also changed throughout the dynasties. The one here refers to a scholar who has passed the commandery-level examinations. ☜

3. This is the more specific term I was talking about in the footnote before this. ☜

Chapter 300: Your Father Was a Diabolic Creed Leader

Hearing what Little Seven had shared, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou instinctively turned to look at Li Haoran with an odd expression.

There seems to be a previous creed leader here.

“Hey hey hey, why are you looking at me?!” Li Haoran hollered.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou withdrew their gazes. True, it's not stipulated that only the Nine-Netherworlds Creed has a previous creed leader. The Radiant Sun Creed and the Heartless Creed aren't ruled out.

Besides, with how poor Qin Haoran was to be mired in debts and hunted down by his creditors, it hardly seems like he's capable of leaving behind treasures.

“Who is Lord Mi? Who is the ‘previous creed leader’ he speaks of? And what is the “treasure left behind?’” Qin Yanyan tossed out a series of questions.

Across the Central Continent, only the Four Great Diabolic Creeds—no, wait, the Three Great Diabolic Creeds—have the position of “creed leader.” Perhaps Lord Mi is a member of the Three Great Diabolic Creeds.

Little Seven was startled by Qin Yanyan for a moment before shaking her head. “I don't know. Lord Mi’s communication with us is one-way, and he has set a restriction on our souls, forcing us to obey his commands. He rarely tells us anything.

“Every time Lord Mi came to collect the yang energy, he would ask us whether anything strange had occurred in Guhuai Town or if we had uncovered anything peculiar.” Little Seven was clueless about Lord Mi’s identity.

Town Mayor Fan was also startled. Despite being aware that the three female ghosts were under the orders of “Lord Mi,” he had no idea that Lord Mi was associated with the Three Great Diabolic Creeds. Had he known, he wouldn't have dared to use the female ghosts for promotional purposes.

No matter how much I yearn for political achievements, I wouldn't dare to have any connection with the Three Great Diabolic Creeds. Along with the eradication of the Everlasting Creed, I've heard that many officials who worked with the Everlasting Creed for the sake of political achievements had been exposed and ousted, sending shockwaves across the imperial court.

Speaking of which, wasn't it the Dao-Seeking Sect that discovered the Everlasting Creed? The Dao-Seeking Sect is indeed one of the Five Great Immortal Sects.

I wonder which big shot tracked down the Everlasting Creed's headquarters.

“Immortal Fairy, do the three of them have restrictions on their souls?” Lu Yang was completely in the dark when it came to matters of souls, so he decided to try consulting the all-knowing Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Yes, but the method used to place the restriction is quite crude, entry-level at best. Should I remove it?”

Lu Yang pondered for a bit. “Will Lord Mi notice?”

“You must be joking. Who do you think I am? Not only is Lord Mi not here, but even if these three female ghosts were right in front of him, he wouldn’t notice that his restriction has been erased!”

“I’ll have to trouble you then, Immortal Fairy.”

When Lu Yang informed the three female ghosts that Lord Mi was related to a diabolic creed, they immediately trembled like leaves in the wind, insisting repeatedly that they were good ghosts and had no connections to any diabolic creed.

Lu Yang smiled. “Of course, I know that you three have no connection to the diabolic creeds. I’m just worried that under Lord Mi’s control, you might be forced to act against your will. And that is why I want to remove your restrictions. From now on, the Dao-Seeking Sect will oversee whether you commit any evil deeds. How does that sound?”

The three female ghosts didn’t dare to refuse and nodded vigorously.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy secretly erased the restriction left by Lord Mi and created a fake one that was completely identical. Anyone at the Fusion Stage and below wouldn’t be able to detect the difference.

The female ghosts instantly felt their souls become lighter as the long-standing restriction weighing on them vanished.

Little Seven timidly raised her hand and asked, “Umm, can we go back now? It’s almost time for class.” They had to give lessons to scholars every day and were dedicated to their duties, always arriving on time.

“Just the right time. We’ve learned enough about the matter for now.” Everyone got ready to leave.

Before departing, Lu Yang reminded Town Mayor Fan, “Town Mayor, the matter of the diabolic creed is of great importance. Please don’t let anyone know that we were here.” Now that they had uncovered traces of a diabolic creed here, they had to take some action before returning.

“That’s a given.” Town Mayor Fan nodded. When it comes to matters related to diabolic creeds, it’s best to leave it to professionals like the Dao-Seeking Sect. A small figure like me shouldn’t get involved.

After bidding goodbye to Town Mayor Fan, the four humans and three ghosts returned to the dilapidated temple. The three female ghosts went to the main hall to conduct their lessons, while the four humans discussed their next steps in a side room.

Earlier, with the town mayor around, it was inconvenient for Li Haoran to mention some things. Now that there were no outsiders, he was free to speak. “Actually, based on what I remember from my past life, I had come to Guhuai Town to hide something. I even severed all karma, spiritual consciousness, and other probing methods to prevent anyone from finding it. It must be a treasure.”

“There’s really a treasure here?”

“Is Lord Mi really from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?”

“Where is the treasure hidden?”

“What is the treasure?”

“You were so poor in your past life, yet you managed to leave behind a treasure?”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou took turns exclaiming in surprise.

Li Haoran rolled his eyes and said in exasperation, “It’s just a memory fragment. I don’t remember it that clearly, but it’s true that there’s something in Guhuai Town.”

“Hang on, what are you three talking about?” Qin Yanyan was completely out of the loop. What treasure? What Nine-Netherworlds Creed?

What does this have to do with my ex-dad?

The trio exchanged glances. Both Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou could see the helplessness in Li Haoran’s eyes.

Lu Yang advised, “Qin Yanyan and Su Yiren will find out about this sooner or later. Rather than hiding it, it’s better to come clean now.” As Qin Yanyan’s uncle[1], I feel that my niece deserves to know the truth.

Meng Jingzhou thought the same.

Li Haoran hesitated for a moment before resolving to tell his ex-daughter the truth about Qin Haoran’s identity. “Actually, your father, Qin Haoran, was the previous creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed...”

As he laid out the entire story, Qin Yanyan’s expression grew increasingly weird. Never would I have guessed that the father I never met was a diabolic creed’s leader, skilled in deception, and burdened with heavy debts.

After quietly listening to the truth about her father, Qin Yanyan let out a long sigh, then revealed a bitter, resigned smile. What else can I do but accept that my father was the creed leader of a diabolic creed?

In truth, she didn’t have much feeling for Qin Haoran. She had grown up with Su Yiren, and to her, 'Qin Haoran' was little more than a symbol bearing the name 'father.'

“Oh, by the way, since your father was a diabolic creed leader, you’ll face restrictions if you choose to enter politics, join the military, or participate in sects’ entrance exams in the future; you won’t pass the political review check,” Lu Yang kindly reminded her. He had recently been brushing up on the Great Xia Dynasty’s laws and had learned a thing or two.

Qin Yanyan, “...”

Thanks so much for your reminder.

Meng Jingzhou chimed in. “Your parents were married for five hundred years. Given your father’s habits, he probably incurred debts during that time too. But don’t worry, your mother didn’t know about the loans he took out, and your father spent all the money on building up the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. According to the law, such debts do not fall under joint marital liability, so your mother doesn’t have to repay it.” Meng Jingzhou was rather knowledgeable about economic laws.

Qin Yanyan, “...”

Thanks so much for your reminder too.

Qin Yanyan could feel the earnest concern from her two uncles.

“In that case, when my father was in a hurry to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and claimed that he wanted to fight for a future for us mother and daughter...”

Li Haoran nodded solemnly. “To increase his loan limit.

“And to improve his ability to withstand the brunt of overdue repayments.”

1. Just to be more specific, the uncle here refers to the older brother of the father. ☜
